# 572 – Going to the Circus – 1

“Are you ready?”  

“I’ve been ready for a while, Bro,” Kanata, who was carrying a bag, replied as if that was obvious. “I wonder, will Sakura need help with her luggage today?”  

“I-I’m sure she’s fine on her own. Since she can see now.”

When they were out and about, Kanata (as overprotective as he was) would often help Sakura with her luggage. In the end, I thought that he was meddling too much and should leave these things, even if they were necessary, to Mika, but my brother was already moving from window to window to go and help her.

Sakura herself happily replied with an “I can take care of that myself,” as she was about to put a bottle of insecticide, which, for whatever reason, was next to the water bottle she was mistaking it for, into her bag. This was a common enough scene. On second thought… it might be better if he did help her.

“By the way, Kanata, how do you think about today’s outing to the circus?”  

“Hm? What do you mean?”  

“Look, you told me how happy you were about showing Sakura nice sights during your previous date, didn’t you? How are your feelings about today?”  

“Huh… well…”

He scratched his cheek with his index finger for some time before continuing, seemingly a bit embarrassed. It probably meant that he was about to voice his thoughts about her.

“I think it’s a good thing. When we went in the past, she wasn’t able to see it.”  

“The last time, huh…? That was about a year after she lost her eyesight. But you and her were only around five at the time. Do you remember that?”  

“I do.”  

“Well, I guess _you_ would.”

It was said that geniuses even remembered the time when they were still in the womb. In any case, thinking back on it, even at that time, Kanata had been helping Sakura.

_That reminds me! He started protecting her right after she lost her vision. I’m pretty sure it began the day after she returned from the hospital._

Back then, they had only been three or four years old. Looking at it another way… he did well watching over his future girlfriend from such a young age. But if Mika and I had gone through the same, we would’ve acted that way, too. Definitely.

“Now that I think about it, didn’t you have checkups today?”

The organization which researched his brain was even open on Sundays. Kanata and Sakura had their checkups there every second Saturday.

“No, or rather, we had them moved to another day.”  

“I see. Well, I guess that was obvious.”

That research institute had their eyes on Kanata, ever since he was born. It had already been 14 years at this point, did they have any results? I couldn’t help thinking that they were plainly trying to get him to join their organization in the future.

_Oops, would you look at the time._

“We should go outside. Shuu and Rir will be here soon.”  

“Right.”

We left the house. The same moment, the door of the neighboring house opened, from where Mika and Sakura emerged.

“You look cute today!”  

“Same goes for you, Ayumu!”  

“”Eh-heh-heh-heh-heh.””

You might wonder “what the hell are you doing?” but this was Mika and I, so it was on par for the course.  

On that note, what was happening on Kanata’s and Sakura’s side?

“I’m pretty sure it’s been ten years since I was at the circus.”  

“You’re right. Back then, you still…”  

“Yeah, I could only enjoy the sounds.”

Only enjoying the sounds… You kinda had to see what was happening in the circus. That said, did Sakura also have memories of when she was four or five years old?

“But today I’ll be able to see it for real!”  

“Yep, that’s great!”

My brother was patting her head, smiling with a profound happiness. She let it happen just as happily. In the past, she kept complaining when her head was stroked, but now she seemed to enjoy it. Maybe she had just been hiding her embarrassment.

“Oh, that looks nice. Ayumu!”  

“Yes, yes.”  

“Eh-heh-heh.”

At her demand, I gave Mika headpats, too. Her hair was as silky and pretty as always.

“…What did we walk in, here?”  

“Woof, it’s a headpat gathering!”

I looked away from Mika, who was hugging me with happily narrowed eyes, to where the voices were coming from. It looked like Shuu and Rir had arrived while we weren’t looking.

“Shuu! Pet me, too!”  

“Fine.”

The newcomers then joined the petting session. The scene of three boyfriends caressing the heads of their girlfriends in front of their homes must’ve looked strange. At least for outsiders. Well, even for those who knew us.

“…Shouldn’t we be on our way already?” Kanata asked after three minutes had passed.

It was a good thing he reminded us, I wouldn’t have stopped on my own.

“You’re right. Shall we go?” I proposed.  

“Ah… Yeah, let’s!”

Mika looked dissatisfied for a moment when I took my hand from her head, but she immediately broke into a smile and was on board with my brother’s suggestion. It looked like Shuu and Rir had also interrupted their petting session.

Still, each couple then linked arms and hands. Then, with Mika and me in the lead, followed by Kanata and Sakura, and finally Shuu and Rir, we started walking.

+++

# 573 – Going to the Circus – 2

“As expected, there are tons of people.”  

“To think so many are buying the ticket on the day of the performance. It’s a good thing we preordered ours.”

We had arrived at a place where we could see the circus tent. A long line of people had formed at the ticket booth and on the path to the entrance of the tent itself. I thought we had left early enough to watch the first performance, but it looked as if we’d have to content with the second.

“Oh, well, let’s get in line.”  

“Woof.”

After showing the girl at the counter our tickets, we joined the end of the long line. A man wearing an acrobat’s outfit with frills around his neck held up a signboard with “the first part is booked out, this is the end of the line” written on it.

“Good thing we brought snacks.”  

“Absolutely!”

We also brought power banks since we didn’t want our phones to run out of charge. Plus, some cheap binoculars, in case we were seated somewhere with a bad view.

The second performance would end around noon, so we didn’t need to bring lunchboxes… or so you’d think. Mika, Sakura, and Rir each made lunches for two people. Indeed, us three boys were quite lucky to have them.

Once the circus performance was over, we’d find seats in a nearby park and eat there. Feeding each other, and all. Maybe we’d also exchange some of our lunches?

“Woof… It feels like there are a lot of gazes on us…!”  

“That’s normal.”  

“It sure is.”

Ever since we were little, people had been staring at us. Especially now with Rir joining us, we were likely the center of attention. That was further helped by the fact that Sakura and Kanata were famous due to that heartwarming documentary about them. It was unavoidable.

“E-Even so, to think so many would look at us.”  

“The six of us haven’t been outside together since we went to welcome Rir. You better get used to it, Sakura,” Mika told her sister. “Especially since you were on TV twice.”  

“Bwuh…”

Come to think of it, both Sanada and Hunkydorky mentioned something like that. On the internet, there apparently were (ongoing) threads titled such as “girl who used to be blind turns out once-in-a-century beauty” and “Kanata (14), caring genius childhood friend with both overly perfect personality and looks.”

In any case, all that fame gave my younger brother and my future sister-in-law a hard time.

“Well, should anything happen, I’ll make sure to protect you.”  

“K-Kanata…! I-I’m happy to hear that, but please say these things when we’re at home.”  

“Alright.”

Maybe we stood out because of our good looks, maybe it was because of Kanata’s and Sakura’s fame, or maybe it was because we flirted and made out even if we were in front of others.

Such thoughts crossed my mind. But in the end, we couldn’t resist hugging each other even when we were outside, so I couldn’t complain.

“Woof, should we play games on our phones?”  

“Those you can play with six people?”

In any case, we had Shuu with us, who’d gotten so strong that there was no one in Japan who’d be a match for him[1](https://re-library.com/translations/levelmaker/volume-19/chapter-573-going-to-the-circus-2/#easy-footnote-bottom-1-117314), so we didn’t have to be overly vigilant.

As Rir had suggested, we linked our phones and started playing games. Well, it was only a digital version of playing cards.

“…Woof, revolution[2](https://re-library.com/translations/levelmaker/volume-19/chapter-573-going-to-the-circus-2/#easy-footnote-bottom-2-117314)!”  

“Wha-!? Seriously?”  

“In that case…”

Kanata had always been in the lead, so he was understandably surprised.

Meanwhile, the circus’ first performance started. One round would take two hours (with a ten-minute break at the halfway point). Afterwards, there’d be a 30-minute break between performances.

In other words, we’d have to wait two hours and 40 minutes until the second performance started. But in exchange we’d be among the first to enter. The six of us could sit at the very front of the unreserved seats.

“Two and a half more hours… I don’t think we can keep playin’ cards all that time.”  

“But time we pass quickly. If we play something.”  

“Guess so.”

All the spectators for the first performance had entered and we were right in front of the tent. We brought our own drinks and snacks, so we didn’t buy anything from the stalls and vendors going around. Correction, Sakura bought some candy bars.

“Oh, look at that! It’s a huge line!”

When I checked where the voice was coming from, I saw a TV crew, including an announcer with a microphone and a crewman holding a large camera.

“Let’s try to get some interviews!”

_Oh, from where this is going, they’ll likely come to us…_

“Could I ask you for an interview?”

_And here they are._

On that note, we (including Shuu, since I often dragged him into it) were interviewed all the time. I had no issues answering questions, no matter who asked, but… with our current group…

“Oh!? Could you be the ones from that documentary…?”

They were closing in on Kanata and Sakura.

“And that’s the foreign student who came here through that program and the son of her foster family! What a lineup of people!”

The cameraman muttered not a moment later.

_What, don’t tell me Mika and I are the only ones with no attention on us? Well, up to this point, it was always-_

“Woah! There’s also the ‘bane of the industry[3](https://re-library.com/translations/levelmaker/volume-19/chapter-573-going-to-the-circus-2/#easy-footnote-bottom-3-117314)‘…”  

“Oh, you’re right! The two who keep refusing all recruitment attempts…”

In the end, all six of us were famous in some way. Still, this was the first time I heard that nickname.

#### Footnotes:

1. Sure, until you get some random punk with a gun.[](https://re-library.com/translations/levelmaker/volume-19/chapter-573-going-to-the-circus-2/#easy-footnote-1-117314)

2. The original is 革命, which doesn’t seem to have any card-game related homophones. No clue if this is an error. It might be meant in the sense of “revolution against the omnipotent Kanata”.[](https://re-library.com/translations/levelmaker/volume-19/chapter-573-going-to-the-circus-2/#easy-footnote-2-117314)

3. The original is 業界殺し (“business world/industry killer”). I changed it slightly.

+++

# 574 – Going to the Circus – 3

“Thank you so much for giving us an interview!” the announcer said, giving us a shallow bow.

Incidentally, it had mostly been Kanata, who was currently famous, answering the question, with only a few words from someone else mixed in here and there. From how the cameraman and other staff-members looked, they’d likely use the whole thing, so I hoped we hadn’t said anything weird.

“Hey there, it’s been a while.”

After the interview was over and most of the TV crew had left, one of them who seemed to be a higher-up came to us.

“Oh… it really has been.”

Mika and I knew this man well. Shuu also, since he had been caught up with him once. And he was also among those who had gathered material about Kanata and Sakura. He usually directed the coverage of incidents.

“By the way…”  

“We refuse.”  

“Yes, what he said.”

Although he wasn’t a talent scout, he always tried to recruit us. Still, once we refused, he backed down right away, so he wasn’t an unpleasant guy.

“Honestly, we could make tons of money if the six of you were to join the TV industry. Well, not me, just the higher-ups.”  

“More importantly, I’m curious about this ‘bane of the industry’ several people of your crew called us earlier…” Mika interjected, voicing what was also bothering me.  

“Oh, that. To be frank, you guys are better looking that most idols and actors. On the internet, there are discussions about the ‘most beautiful sisters of the generation’ and threads like ‘after finding the most beautiful girl in the world, another one appeared in the same neighborhood’.”

“Huh, that’s what they saw about me?” Mika asked.  

“And me!?” I added.  

“What, you didn’t know?”

Seeing we never even once appeared on TV, this came as a surprise… was what I’d like to say, but what would be a lie. Still, we were just regular people who happened to be with Kanata and the others when they were interviewed. I didn’t know if people made photos of us in secret, but it wasn’t a possibility I could exclude. Not when we were involved.

“Moreover, if we managed to get you to join the industry, we’d undoubtedly make billions… or even trillions. But you keep refusing, so you’re now called the ‘bane of the industry’… Oh, would you look at the time. I should go back to my work. Just think about it, will you? I’m sure you don’t need my business card at this point. See you.”

The director made his way back to the TV crew from earlier. Mika and I breathed a sigh, while Kanata, Sakura, and Shuu looked as if this had been the most normal thing in the world.

Rir, however…

“W-Woof… he tried to recruit you!”

She showed quite a strong reaction[1](https://re-library.com/translations/levelmaker/volume-19/chapter-574-going-to-the-circus-3/#easy-footnote-bottom-1-117316), given this had been the first time for her.

“Rir, you were included in that offer right now, y’know?”  

“W-W-W-Woof!!? Are you serious!?”  

“Ah-ha-ha… I am, least ’bout that.”

The man had definitely talked about all six of us. I mean, Shuu had the looks of an action movie actor and Rir was currently closing in on second place of our school’s “most beautiful girls ranking” (though for some reason, this was under the assumption of “excluding Ayumu”).

“I’m not that beautiful or cute…!”  

“You gotta face reality.”  

“W-Woof~.” With her cheeks bright red, she threw herself at Shuu. She was trembling like a frightened puppy.

Well, it gave us ample things to talk about while we were waiting, so the interview had its upsides.

“Ha-ha-ha… With how things are going, we’ll be the ones who get picked for the performances with audience participation.”  

“Don’t say that… it might actually happen.”

Kanata’s joke sounded like something that could really happen to us.

“…There’s still two hours left.”  

“Still this long, huh?”

All of us, other than Rir, had calmed down from the interview, so we put down a mat, spread out our snacks, and started to eat them. There were several families doing the same.

“Oh! It’s Long-Heart!” a little girl behind us yelled.

Long-Heart was a clown who acted as the circus’ mascot. He wore super-thick make-up, so it was hard to guess his original facial features. He was quite active and showed up occasionally on TV shows and during prime time, when the circus performed around Tokyo. He never spoke and only communicated via captions.

That wasn’t all, he also posted videos titled “Long-Heart’s[2](https://re-library.com/translations/levelmaker/volume-19/chapter-574-going-to-the-circus-3/#easy-footnote-bottom-2-117316) Daily Life” on movie platforms and the circus’ official website. The total views apparently exceeded a million. For that reason, there were many people who’d never attended the circus’ performance but knew about him.

“Oh, you’re right! It’s Long-Heart!”  

“Long Heart~!”

They probably wanted to entertain the guests who were waiting for the second performance. That’s why they brought him out.

He took position a bit removed from the long line and demonstrated backflips. People obviously clapped and cheered at everything he did. Even the six of us, who hadn’t been fans of him so far, were mesmerized and applauded like the others.

It was as if his skill drew us in. It was incredible.

Long-Heart started to simply juggle cueballs. Then he looked up and threw them dangerously high, though it was likely on purpose.

_…Huh? Now that I get a closer look at him, haven’t I seen this face before somewhere?_

#### Footnotes:

1. The original is 反能, which isn’t a proper word. This is likely a mistyped 反応 (“reaction”).[](https://re-library.com/translations/levelmaker/volume-19/chapter-574-going-to-the-circus-3/#easy-footnote-1-117316)

2. “Love-Long” in the original. There are tons of typos/errors with this character (calling him Heart-Long” instead of “Long-Heart” for example) so I won’t make a footnote for every instance.[](https://re-library.com/translations/levelmaker/volume-19/chapter-574-going-to-the-circus-3/#easy-footnote-2-117316)

+++

# 575 – Long-Heart

_Where was it… I can’t tell with all that clown make-up. I can’t imagine him being Mr. Mitsuo, since his dandy looks don’t fit this mascot._

Now he started spinning plates. He balanced a white plate on a stick and started rotating it. But then he dropped it, likely on purpose.

Just for a moment, it evoked dejected shouts. Incidentally, Rir’s and Sakura’s were among them.

Still, this was a circus. The moment the plate hit the ground – maybe because it was made of rubber – it bounced back up and into Long-Heart’s hands.

“Incredible, this is quite a difficult trick. To bounce it right back even though it’s spinning.”  

“You’re right…”

It was amazing… To be blunt, while all of us, except for Rir, where here the second time, the first had been ten years ago, so I’d forgotten almost everything other than the really impressive stuff. What I was seeing right now felt new.

There was clapping and cheering. I obviously also joined in.

“Oh, looks like it’s not over yet!”  

“The service here is incredible.”

Now Long-Heart was taking out something like darts. A troupe member who’d been selling stuff earlier appeared some distance away from Long-Heart with five inflated balloons on their waist.

“He’s going to pop them from this distance? Though I guess we could manage that easily.”  

“Some skills are effective even on this side, Kanata, you can’t use as a comparison! Hmph!”  

“Bro, please don’t puff out your cheeks… I get what you mean.”

“There!”  

“Mph-”

Mika put her hands on my puffed-out cheeks and forced me to expel the air. Was that how a burst balloon felt?

“Aw, he missed…” Rir shouted after the first throw.

Well, it was obviously staged. The second throw also missed like the first. And the third…

“Oh”

The third dart finally hit the balloon and burst it. Long-Heart was jumping in apparent delight.  

The fourth throw also hit. The balloon burst with a satisfying pop.

“Oh, looks like they’re increasing the distance.”

Both the salesperson and Long-Heart stepped back from their positions and the latter readied his darts again. They were quite far apart. Well, it still was a distance you often enough saw on TV shows.

Then, he threw darts with both hands. Each of them spectacularly popped one balloon.

“Woof! That just now was amazing!”  

“Yep, this is a circus, after all!”

Yes, it would’ve been difficult already to just hit with one of them, so to hit two at the same time was quite the feat. But on second thought, this was also something you regularly saw on TV. Though experiencing it in person made a big difference.

“They’re increasing the distance even more!?” one of the spectators shouted.

Long-Heart signaled the salesperson to step back even further and then took quite some distance himself, too. He was getting pretty close to us.

“No way, this distance ain’t gonna work,” Shuu muttered.

He’d been commenting on quite a few things earlier, which told me that he had fun.

I suddenly felt that something was off and used the zoom on my phone’s camera to look at the salesperson.

“Is something wrong, Ayumu? Are you making a video in case he succeeds?  

“Well, not exactly…”

As long as it wasn’t inside the tent, people were generally allowed to make recordings. But that wasn’t what I was going for. For some reason, I had the feeling that the staff members were just as surprised as the guests. A hunch… which turned out to be true.

The salesperson who assisted with the performance looked shocked. The other staff members who surrounded Long-Hart at some distance also seemed surprised at him further increasing the distance. I could tell that their expressions were genuine. Was Long-Hart attempting something that hadn’t been planned in advance?

The clown started to rotate his arms in a large, deliberate motion. Then, he took the stance of a baseball pitcher and threw just the dart’s needle. It flew without losing speed and it soon hit the balloon the salesperson, who was standing quite far away, was holding.

“Woah~, incredible~!!”

Loud cheers rose. I myself felt like shouting. It was incredible, truly amazing! To reach it at that distance. People were taking photos and recording videos.

When I looked back at the salesperson, they had a genuine blank look on their face. It seemed as if it hadn’t been arranged in advance, after all.

Unaware of his colleagues’ shock, Long-Heart now pulled a pink balloon from his pocket. He attached it to the nozzle of a container likely filled with helium gas, which he was carrying on his waist, and inflated the balloon. Then he twisted it several times, creating the standard balloon-dog.

He tied a string around it, put his hand to his forehead, and then started searching the audience for children. Said children were obviously looking excited. Well, none of our group looked like a child, so he surely wouldn’t pick us.

The moment I had that thought, the clown’s head stopped turning when he saw us, and he briskly walked our way. Finally, he pointed at Sakura.  

Looking surprised, she pointed at herself. The clown nodded.

Since she had been chosen, Sakura stepped forward and accepted the balloon-dog.

That moment…! That moment it happened! Long-Heart looked at me. Not just once or twice… but three times with a truly shocked expression on his face. Finally, he spoke with a voice that was somewhat muffled but still laced with surprise.

“Could it be… that you’re Alim!?”

---

**TL notes:**  

What a huge surprise! Who could’ve guessed the overly talented clown was Mephistophales? Seems like he also brought some skills over from Anazumu.

For those who’ve read the LN; this chapter has lots of similarities to volume 2’s eBook bonus story. While there might be future chapters featuring his tricks, my guess is that the bonus story was mostly based on this chapter.

+++

# 576 – The Circus Leader – 1

“Bwuh?”

I could only assume that I also had a shocked look on my face. All given, this man had to be Aichou Mitsuo. To think the very leader of the troupe would act as the mascot… Hang on, wasn’t that pretty common?

“Ah, uhm, if you aren’t who I thought you were, please forget what I said.”  

“N-No, you got it right.”

The five others with me also looked utterly shocked, likely a combination of not knowing what was going on and someone who knew about Anazumu suddenly appearing. With all that going on, Kanata probably was about to freeze up.

“I see… I see! To think we’d meet again so soon… the gods really might still be with us. My apologies, we should continue this talk later. Hang on, where was it again?”

Mr. Mitsuo searched his pockets for a notebook and a ball-point-pen, quickly scribbling something onto a page and handing that to me.

“Please come to that location by yourself in 15 minutes.”  

“Understood.”

After seeing me agree, he returned to the other guests with a somewhat relieved look on his face.

_Now, I’ll have to explain things to everyone._

“Bro, what was that just now…?”  

“Hm? The leader of this circus troupe… in other words, the person playing Long-Heart, has been to Anazumu.”  

“What!?”

Four of them heard about this for the first time, so their shock was understandable. Mika also seemed to have forgotten about it.

“Eh… when did you ever… I don’t remember anyone other than us coming to Anazumu…”  

“You have met him, Mika.”  

“I have?”  

“Yup.”

Well, she didn’t have any contact with Mr. Mitsuo afterwards and we never brought him up in conversation, plus in the first place we had to bring all the dead back to life with Amritas, so it was only natural she forgot about him.

“He was one of the demons who attacked the Mephilad Kingdom-”  

“Oh~!!? Don’t tell me he was this Mephisto-Something guy?”  

“Exactly.”

It looked like she did remember him. That would make this quick.

“That man was apparently trying to return to Earth, so he conspired with the demons, but he was captured by the kingdom and sentenced to death.”  

“I remember now. To think that was him.”  

“Yep. I snuck into the castle and brought back a part of his body, which I used to revive him.”

Afterwards, I told the other four, who didn’t know the rest of the story, what kind of man Mr. Mitsuo was and what he had done.

“Was it really fine to let this guy return to Earth? Won’t he start committin’ crimes?”  

“I put emphasis on that when I sent him back and even considered brainwashing him to some extent[1](https://re-library.com/translations/levelmaker/volume-19/chapter-576-the-circus-leader-1/#easy-footnote-bottom-1-117444)…”  

“Brainwashin’…”

At that, Shuu flinched back slightly. Sure, it was a cruel option, but in the end, it was the safest one.

“Still… to think someone from Earth arrived in Anazumu more than a hundred years before you, Bro. But this Mr. Mitsuo did. And now he’s running the circus… It sounds like the time he arrived after being sent back was random.”

Indeed, the man had lived for more than a hundred years, but no matter how you sliced it, he looked like someone from our parents’ generation. It was truly strange… maybe Kanata was right with his assumption that he arrived at a random time when I sent him back.

“I-In that case, weren’t we super lucky that we arrived at a point in time when you were also there, Big Sis, Ayu-nii??”  

“Woof, if Shuu had arrived at a different point in time… I would’ve ended up violated by countless men…”

Sakura nuzzled up to Mika, while Rir hugged Shuu with an anxious expression. The two huggees let it happen without protest.

“Even assuming it was fate that brought you and Shuu together, Rir, it feels like us reuniting with Bro and Mika-nee was inevitable.”  

“You’re right, Kanata. I feel the same,” Mika agreed.

My watch showed that Mr. Mitsuo’s 15 minutes had passed. His show as Long-Heart was already over.

“I’ll be going, then.”  

“…Should we come with you?” Mika asked worriedly.  

“No, I’m the only one who has a deeper connection to him, well, and Mika to some extent, so you should stay here. We can talk to him as a group at a later time. For now, just I will go.”  

“That’s probably true. Alright.”

For some reason, Mika seemed worried when she looked at me, but it didn’t feel like there was any need for concern.

I parted with the five of them and followed the concise map Mr. Mitsuo had drawn. Shortly later, I could see what looked like an office outside the circus tent. As expected, there were tons of staff members around. A handsome man – either a foreigner or someone of mixed race – noticed my arrival and closed in on me.

“What’s wrong, missy? Did you get lost?”

As usually, people assumed I was a girl. Well, that didn’t matter at the moment.

“No, uhm… I was invited here by Mr. Aichou Mitsuo.”  

“Mitsuo[2](https://re-library.com/translations/levelmaker/volume-19/chapter-576-the-circus-leader-1/#easy-footnote-bottom-2-117444)? The boss invited you here!? Right, now that you mention it, when he came back from entertaining the people in line earlier, he did say ‘I’m currently waiting for an important guest, so when she arrives, please let her through. You’ll know her when you see her, she’s ridiculously pretty.’ I guess that’s you! Alright, come with me.”

The man would apparently show me in.

#### Footnotes:

1. The original is closer to “I did some brainwashing, so I think it’ll be fine”. The problem is that for all we know, he didn’t, so I translated it this way. Does threatening someone count as brainwashing in Japan?[](https://re-library.com/translations/levelmaker/volume-19/chapter-576-the-circus-leader-1/#easy-footnote-1-117444)

2. The man uses Katakana for some words, likely to indicate that he’s a foreigner with an accent (he uses ジャポン at one point, so it’s possible he’s from a French-speaking country). This is also the first time it is confirmed that 光夫 is read as “Mitsuo”.[](https://re-library.com/translations/levelmaker/volume-19/chapter-576-the-circus-leader-1/#easy-footnote-2-117444)

+++

# 577 – The Circus Leader – 2

“Yo, Boss! The girl you mentioned earlier is here!”

This was most likely the room of the troupe leader. I looked more frugal than expected… but on second thought, everything had to be movable, so that was probably natural. Mr. Mitsuo was sitting in front of a mirror, likely to fix his clown makeup.

“Sorry for the trouble and thank you for showing her in.”  

“It’s all good. You sure are a smooth operator to hook up with such an angel, Boss. Did you discover her while you went outside yesterday? What were relationships with minors called again in Japan? Paid dating[1](https://re-library.com/translations/levelmaker/volume-19/chapter-577-the-circus-leader-2/#easy-footnote-bottom-1-117446)?”

_P-Paid dating…? There’s no way I’d ever prostitute myself! Not for women and definitely not for men! Not in a thousand years!_

“Perish the thought, we are mere acquaintances. I called her here for a small matter.”  

“Huh, I see. That’s fine, then. I’m going back outside.”

The troupe member who’d shown me in left the room.

“My apologies for that, please have a seat.”  

“Of course.”

I didn’t know if it was intended for guests, but I sat down on a wooden bench. Mr. Mitsuo reached a good point to finish applying make-up and sat down in a chair opposite me. His face obviously still looked like that of a clown.

“Come to think of it, don’t you have to be on stage all the time as a clown…?” I asked, since I was curious about that part.  

“No need to worry. It will be some more time until I have to leave, I should still have around 15 minutes.”  

“I see.”

It felt strange to see a clown, who’d earlier been joking around, talk seriously about something. Even more so one who was famous on TV and such.

“Before we talk, do you mind if I smoke?”  

“Eh… please do.”

Mr. Mitsue took out a box, pressed down on its edge and tried to take a cigarette from it. However, due to some contraption, it wouldn’t come out right and instead was shot by a spring right into his face.

“Ouch!”  

“Heh-heh-ha-ha!”

I couldn’t help laughing at what looked like a deliberate joke.

“It’s been like this since I returned yesterday.”  

“I see… Does that mean when I sent you home from Anazumu…”  

“Indeed, I arrived yesterday on Earth’s calendar[2](https://re-library.com/translations/levelmaker/volume-19/chapter-577-the-circus-leader-2/#easy-footnote-bottom-2-117446).”

The one who arrived more than a hundred years before us in Anazumu returned to Earth only yesterday… was that what they called a time paradox? A scary thought.

“Heh-heh, but thanks to that, all my skills and memories as a circus clown… and the troupe leader came back.”  

“Oh, I get it! When you move between Anazumu and Earth, you bring your memories with you… but they feel different.”  

“Exactly.”

It sounded like it was the same for him. Although he’d been an awfully long time in the other world, he still remembered how to use electric devices. How strange.

“…I ended up getting ahead of myself. Miss Alim Nariwei, I welcome you to my circus!”  

“Eh-heh-heh, that really was a coincidence!”  

“Almost as if it had been planned.”

Still, when people here called me Alim, I assumed it was related to my game handle. Well, I’d get used to it with time.

“I’m… not sure how to thank you…”  

“As I said before, just don’t commit any crimes on this side.”  

“Being executed took a great toll on me. I am only too aware of that.”

As I was thinking that I had seen his clown face somewhere other than on TV, I realized that it was the same he had as Mephistophales[3](https://re-library.com/translations/levelmaker/volume-19/chapter-577-the-circus-leader-2/#easy-footnote-bottom-3-117446). A clown enemy… that was something straight out of a video game or movie.

“Well, in any case, Miss Alim… or rather, you were called Ayumu on this side, right? It is rare to see a girl with that name. On a closer look, your face has barely changed. Are the only differences the color of your hair and skin, and your height due to your age?”  

“No, my gender is also different.”

The clown – someone who was skilled at surprising people and making them laugh – now looked rather surprised himself. He cautiously opened his mouth and spoke again.

“Eh… what, does that mean you are currently male…?  

“Yes, I am a boy.”  

“…Eh? I mean, what!? No matter how I look at you, you seem to be female… even your voice…”  

“Well, I’m male in my family register and I have all the right body parts. On Earth, that is. People are usually shocked by that.”

I myself was getting a thrill out of surprising others. It was fun to reveal my gender to them, so I usually did it myself. But with my face and voice, people tended to treat me like a girl, so I had to be careful.

“So, your gender differs between here and over there…!”  

“It does.”  

“Then, which one is your true gender?”  

“The one here.”

For some reason, his surprise seemed to turn into admiration. But I couldn’t guess what kind of admiration that was.

“I-In any case, Mr. Ayumu. I wanted to thank you, so I spent several hours yesterday thinking of something…”  

“It’s fine, no need to go to extremes.”  

“No, I absolutely want to show you my gratitude! Otherwise, I won’t be able to settle down!”

_From the way he talks, it’s probably better to accept. I wonder what he has for me. I get the feeling that it’ll be related to the circus, though…_

“I’ll go get it, please wait a moment,” he said and then left the room in the silly gait typical of a clown.

#### Footnotes:

1. The man calls it エンコー (enkoo), an abbreviation of 援助交際 (“paid dating”), which is apparently a method for underage girls to prostitute themselves in Japan. I couldn’t find a good way to abbreviate the English name, so I left it as it is.[](https://re-library.com/translations/levelmaker/volume-19/chapter-577-the-circus-leader-2/#easy-footnote-1-117446)

2. While I no longer trust the author to keep even the simplest of numbers straight, I assume this is deliberate. Which would indicate that Jizou puppeteered him around for more than a week.[](https://re-library.com/translations/levelmaker/volume-19/chapter-577-the-circus-leader-2/#easy-footnote-2-117446)

3. I was gonna snark about that, but I guess he only saw him twice with the clown make-up (during Karua’s rescue and the war) which was months ago, so it’s understandable that he didn’t recognize the face immediately.[](https://re-library.com/translations/levelmaker/volume-19/chapter-577-the-circus-leader-2/#easy-footnote-3-117446)

+++

# 578 – Lifetime VIP Free-Pass

“Here you go.”

He handed me two cards. They had “Love Long Circus Lifetime VIP Free-Pass” written on them, plus a note saying, “If anyone at the counter is shown this card, they are to immediately call the troupe leader.”

“If you show one of these cards, you and up to nine others may attend the performance free of charge. Furthermore, you’ll be shown to special seats with added service.”  

“Eh… uhm… okay?”

I could understand that much from what was written on them.

“My apologies, most people don’t visit the same circus that often in their lives[1](https://re-library.com/translations/levelmaker/volume-19/chapter-578-lifetime-vip-free-pass/#easy-footnote-bottom-1-117448)… but that was all I could currently prepare,” he explained in a truly apologetic tone. “Even though I caused you so much trouble and owe you a much greater gratitude.”  

“Uhm, thank you very much…?”  

“As soon as I can think of another way to thank you, I will… Oh, I’ll also give you my contact information.”

I didn’t know where he was going with this, but he gave me his social media contacts and phone number. He then looked at the clock.

“We’ll also reimburse you for what you paid for your tickets later and you’ll be invited to special seats as it says on the card during the next performance.”  

“Huh, are you sure? Sorry for the trouble.”

_This probably isn’t something I should refuse. Definitely. Since we have the chance, we should make use of it… But as he said earlier, you only go to the circus once every few years at best. Oh, well._

“I still have some time… uhm, would you mind if I asked a few questions?”  

“Of course. As long as it isn’t anything strange.”

_Like personal details about us. Ugh… I remember some creep asking about my bust and waist size. In any case, it’s fine as long as it’s not stuff like that._

“You noticed I gave you two of these cards, right? They are also meant as an apology. Since you told me that you returned to this side, there was this other girl I killed by accident… did she come with you today?”  

“Yes, she did! She was standing next to me earlier. A girl with long, black hair and otherworldly beauty.  

“It feels like among your friends there were several girls with otherworldly beauty… I see, so she’s the one with long, black hair.”

Normally, referring to Mika as a “girl with otherworldly beauty” or some similar descriptor would be enough for anyone to get who I meant, but, unfortunately, Sakura and Rir were with us today… and Kanata too, I suppose. Since there were several options, I added the part about her hair.

“Still, I see. When I met you for the first time, I assumed she was a close friend of the same gender, but in truth you are male, Mr. Ayumu, so that means…”  

“Well, yes, it’s what you assume.”

Mr. Mitsuo gave a nod with strangely satisfied expression.

“Also… when I called your name, it wasn’t just you and… Miss Mika. I remember the others of your group also being surprised. I first assumed that was because a clown who normally doesn’t talk spoke to them, but it seems that wasn’t it…”

_Oh, he noticed._

“Moreover, that girl with white hair…” he continued. “For some reason, I feel like I’ve seen the color often in Anazumu.”  

“Yes, you’re right. All six of us have a connection with the other world.”  

“What, really?!”

His clown face was tinged with astonishment. In my opinion, he acted a bit too shocked. It was probably better to tell him more details.

“Among the group, one is my best friend since we were little, one is my younger brother, and another one Mika’s younger sister. All three were, by complete coincidence, summoned as sages to defeat an evil god different from Samaeyl.”  

“To think… that just those close to you were gathered. You could only call this an extreme coincidence. So… the girl with white hair…”  

“She became my best friend’s girlfriend while he was in Anazumu and we brought her here with us.”  

“S-Such a thing is possible!? No wonder she seems so out of place on Earth.”  

“Yes, it’s possible.”

From her appearance, Rir was seen as a normal (if very beautiful) foreigner. Her eyes had the same azure blue they had in Anazumu. This was a color that also naturally existed on Earth. Still, her blueish-white hair wasn’t a something you could have without dyeing it. The story was apparently that some illness had affected it. In other words, her looks had an Anazuman quality.

What would happen if someone with green hair crossed over?

“I see… From what I could gather from the literature over there, there were other people in Anazumu connected to different worlds, but only one every few decades or even centuries. To think there were seven people, including myself… Well, at this point, I am no longer part of the equation.”

Seven transmigrators at the same time certainly sounded like a lot. I never read any historical literature in Anazumu after learning what fell under common knowledge, so I had no idea[2](https://re-library.com/translations/levelmaker/volume-19/chapter-578-lifetime-vip-free-pass/#easy-footnote-bottom-2-117448).

Mr. Mitsuo looked at the clock again. His expression immediately changed.

“My apologies, I will have to leave.”  

“I understand!”  

“I shall do my very best, so I hope you enjoy the next performance.”  

“Of course.”

#### Footnotes:

1. Probably depends on the person. I know some who make habit of visiting the same circus whenever it performs nearby, and even if it’s only once every few years, it adds up with time.[](https://re-library.com/translations/levelmaker/volume-19/chapter-578-lifetime-vip-free-pass/#easy-footnote-1-117448)

2. What good is having a device with millions of digital books and a search function if you never use it?[](https://re-library.com/translations/levelmaker/volume-19/chapter-578-lifetime-vip-free-pass/#easy-footnote-2-117448)

+++

# 579 – VIP Treatment

“The second performance will now start~!” the voice of an older girl resounded.

We could enter the tent at last.

“Finally.”  

“I was more shocked about this circus’ leader being connected to Anazumu than the long wait time. Waiting in line didn’t bother me that much.”  

“That’s true.”

In any case, while the five of them did have their complaints, we entered the tent for now and looked for the best unreserved seats.

“Here looks good.”  

“Those seem to be the best. I had no idea there were such great seats in the unreserved section.”

We quickly sat down so others wouldn’t snatch them up. There was a division between the unreserved and reserved section and the former seats were generally further behind, but the ones we found were almost right in front of the stage.

It was getting close to winter and cold outside, but the tent was warm thanks to an elaborate air conditioning system. Exactly the right temperature to spend two hours here. We took off our jackets and such and placed them in baskets that were installed under the seats.

“…I guess I’ll buy some ice cream later.”  

“Sakura, didn’t you eat candy bars earlier? And now you want ice cream? Besides, isn’t it a bit too cold for that?” Mika chided her.  

“Grr, it’ll be fine. I want to eat some!”

On the way, we had passed salespeople who’d apparently walk around and sell stuff like ice cream. That was part of the service.

“Huh? Is that guy comin’ our way?”  

“Eh?”

As Shuu had said, it seemed like a troupe member was rushing towards us from the stage. Or rather, he was looking at me, doing his utmost to smile. It was him… the foreigner who’d showed me to Mr. Mitsuo’s office.

Shortly later, he came to a stop in the corridor between seats right next to ours. My friends were a given, but even other people around us stared at him, wondering what was going on. I was the only one who knew the reason.

“Uhm… is there an issue?”  

“The six of you are here as a group?”  

“Y-Yes, we are, but…”

As usual, it was Kanata, the most mature among us, who replied. After looking at me, the man’s smile widened even further.

“The boss told me about it. Could you show me the card?”  

“Huh, the card…? Who are you…” Kanata stammered.  

“Ah, yes… Here you go,” I interrupted my brother and held out one of the cards I’d been given.

The man looked at it and nodded. The other five seemed even more confused. I wanted to surprise them, so I had kept mum about the VIP seats. Heh-heh-heh.

“Right, that’s genuine! In that case, I shall show the six of you to your seats.”  

“Y-You’ll show us to our seats?”  

“Yep, he means he’ll guide us to the VIP seats. This card I got earlier as thanks has all kind of perks.”  

“The hell? Why not tell us earlier!?”  

“Ah-ha-ha, I wanted to surprise you.”

It wasn’t every day you got the chance to nab the best unreserved seats, so the others… well, mostly Kanata, were reluctant to get up and part with them. There were some complaints, too. Sorry~.

The troupe member entered the section for reserved seats. We obviously followed him and when he came to a stop, we did the same.

“It’s here.”  

“Woof! What great seats!”

They were probably the best ones in the whole reserved section. I had no idea how they were available, but it was patent how good they were. To begin with, they had a different color from the other seats.

“These are the VIP seats. The boss told me that you saved his life yesterday! That’s awesome, thank you so much! Ever since the circus was established, these seats were meant for people offering substantial loans… or so I heard!”  

“Seats meant for people who loaned the circus a ton of money… that should be fine, no?”

Urged on by the troupe member, we sat down. I didn’t know if Kanata was completely happy with it, but his mood seemed to have improved. These chairs appeared to be the only cushioned ones, which made the difference even more obvious.

“A troupe member will bring you refreshments, do you have any wishes? You may choose anything from the menu. Ever so often, someone will come here in case there is anything you need. At those times, please order anything you want from the menu, like popcorn or ice cream. That’s the service we offer.”  

“Wow, really!?”

Sakura, with her sweet tooth, beamed after being given the menu and hearing what the man just said. She was probably planning to order the popcorn with caramel filling.

In any case, the story was apparently that I saved Mr. Mitsuo’s life. On Earth, that is. Well, it wasn’t that far off the truth, so I didn’t mind.

“I never thought this could happen.”  

“Ah-ha-ha, but isn’t this great?”  

“Well, I guess.”

It looked like there were some things Mika wanted to say, but for now she seemed to agree.

In any case, Sakura immediately ordered an extra-large melon soda and a large serving of caramel popcorn. Mika hurriedly turned her way when she noticed and forced her to reduce both orders by one size. Kanata watched the scene with a grin.

It looked like Shuu and Rir chose something with beef jerky.

_Now, what should I take?_

+++

# 580 – The Love Long Circus – 1

«Now, let’s have fun, everyone! Fill this place with love! Love, love, love – the Love Long Circus!»

The drinks and snacks we had ordered were brought to us ten minutes after the fact. There was a buzzing sound, like the ones you always heard in movie theaters and playhouses. Then, the circus’ theme song played.

“It’s finally starting!”  

“I’m excited what we’ll see!”

Mika and I were holding hands over our seats’ armrests. On that note, all three couples were holding hands with their respective partners. Well, this was pretty much a triple date.

«Everyone, we welcome you to the love-filled Love Long Circus!»

We could hear the voice of the girl doing commentary from speakers.

«From near and far you’ve come, thank you so much for visiting us! We hope you enjoy these dreamlike two hours overflowing with love!»

Mr. Mitsuo, or rather, Long-Heart walked onto the stage with unsteady steps, carrying something that looked like a tire.

«Long-Heart has arrived! It looks like he wants to greet everyone!»

The clown dropped the tire and looked around while waving at the audience from the stage. He was famous even outside the circus, so the spectators were extremely excited. Even Mika seemed hyped up and gripped my hand more strongly. Her eyes were shining as she gazed at the stage.

_Hang, I should look at the stage, not Mika. Since we came here to watch the circus._

«What’s that? Long-Heart is going to demonstrate a trick to greet everyone…? He is! Long-Heart will balance on the tire!»

People were clapping and cheering, even though nothing had happened yet.

Mr. Mitsuo… no, Long-Heart placed the tire on the floor upright and then climbed onto it. The moment he did (as would happen to anyone who tried that) he crashed down face-first. The tire fell to the ground next to him and he flailed his arms and legs in apparent frustration. He then made a gesture meaning, “once more” and put the tire upright again.

When he tried to climb on it once more, he tumbled down again. He then stood up and stamped his feet in vexation, before crossing his arms to (feign to) think. About five seconds later, together with a sound-effect from the speakers, he acted as if he had an idea and picked the tire up a third time.

Finally, he… didn’t climb on it like before, instead he made a handstand on it. It was something new, and he had succeeded on the first attempt.

“Wha-… incredible!?”  

“Woof, even I couldn’t do that…!”  

“As expected from a circus performer.”

No matter how you looked at it, doing a handstand on a tire was more difficult than what he tried earlier. Long-Heart alighted from the tire, nodded a few times in apparent satisfaction and then tried to climb onto it like earlier. However, he failed once more.

One way succeeded while the other failed. I couldn’t help bursting out laughing.

“He’s good at making people laugh… Ha-ha!”  

“The circus is so much fun, Kanata!” Sakura cheered.  

“Well, it feels like I’m here for the first time, too,” my brother replied.

Both circus first-timers seemed to be having fun. Rir also got excited like a little child and ended up being tangled up with Shuu.

“I wonder if the performances got better since we were here the last time,” Mika mused.  

“It was ten years ago, so I don’t remember it clearly. Still… it feels like you’re right.”

Long-Heart inclined his head as if to say “huh?”, then picked up the tire and put it around his neck, before giving the audience a bow and leaving the stage.

«Long-Heart will be back! Now, the first performance will be ‘Airial Acrobatics’. Watch as they deftly manipulate fabric suspended from above and use it to perform lovely dances!»

As the woman had said, fabric was lowered from the tent’s roof. Several performers who wore outfits like those of ballet dancers appeared and bowed to the audience.

The lighting[1](https://re-library.com/translations/levelmaker/volume-19/chapter-580-the-love-long-circus-1/#easy-footnote-bottom-1-117502) changed, transforming the tent’s interior and the atmosphere into something graceful. Each of the performers put their feet on the cloth, and once the music started, they climbed up swiftly while rolling it up.

“Woof~, they’re climbing so dexterously.”  

“That somethin’ you could do, Rir?”  

“Doing a handstand on a tire might still be possible, but not this. Not even wolfkin can do everything.”  

“Makes sense.”

No matter how far Rir’s athletic abilities outstripped those of normal people (according to the girls, she was incredibly good in PE), even she couldn’t move her body completely as she wanted. Well, that was natural. Shuu, another monster in regard to athletic ability, couldn’t do the stuff circus performers did either.

“Hm~, that’s how a circus should be!”  

“You’re right…”

It was indeed lovely how they repeatedly climbed the cloth, descended it, and climbed it once more.

_And there are still many more performances to come. I can’t help feeling excited._

#### Footnotes:

1. The original is 証明 (“proof”, “verification”). I assume that’s an error and meant to be the homophone 照明 (“lighting”, “illumination”).[](https://re-library.com/translations/levelmaker/volume-19/chapter-580-the-love-long-circus-1/#easy-footnote-1-117502)

+++

# 581 – The Love Long Circus – 2

After the aerial acrobatics came three people who looked like gymnasts and performed chair-climbing tricks. They piled the chairs up higher and higher, always keeping their balance.

Once that was over, Long-Heart made another appearance. He’d apparently show up every two acts to entertain the audience. In the end, he _was_ the poster clown of the circus.

«Next, guiding the elephants will be-»

It sounded like the next part would involve elephants. When it came to circuses, it was all about the animals. Rare animals like white tigers would apparently also make their appearance. Would we get to see them jump through rings of fire?

Putting that aside, it was now the turn of the elephants. There were three of them led by their trainer.

“Woah… Elephants! It’s real elephants!”  

“Oh, right. This is the first time you see those in person, right, Sakura? Should we go to the zoo on our next date?”  

“Yeah, let’s do that.”

Sakura was happily leaning against Kanata’s shoulder. You didn’t see her do that often. Well, they probably acted intimately when there were no others around.  

_Are they happy together? Alright, I should bring it up, too._

“Mika, should we also go to the zoo on our next date? On a day when we won’t run into Kanata and Sakura.”  

“Alright, let’s do that!”

_Great, I managed to settle that while we’re here._

In any case, the elephant show was also incredible.

_I mean, if it’s normal stuff… what ordinary people can do, then I can pull that off in Anazumu any time, but animal handling is outside of my expertise. I can’t help being genuinely impressed._

One of the elephants painted a simple picture on a canvas, another climbed onto a box that looked physically too small to do that, and the last used his own trunk like a hula hoop. Then, they suddenly combined their powers and formed a pyramid (one made so it wouldn’t put needless strain on their bodies) and caught balls. Hopefully, all that wasn’t too hard on their trunks.

On that note, there was apparently a corner where you could meet the animals after the circus performances were over. Still, one of Rir’s wolflike traits – her keen sense of smell – was present even on Earth, and while it wasn’t as bad as with dogs who could no longer control themselves, it seemed to be hard on her. As a consequence, she and Shuu would wait outside. It was a pity.

«Those were the elephants Flower, Blossom, and Yoshio!»

The elephant show was over. The names Flower and Blossom were obvious, but I had no idea where Yoshio was from.

The next part would apparently consist of motorcycles driving around inside an iron sphere.

______  

____  

__

“Woof, next will be the highlight! Trapeze swinging in mid-air!”

After the motorcycles came juggling (with throwing knives), followed by magic tricks, and finally, as Rir had said, trapeze swinging, the highlight of the show. There were three things you thought of when it came to circuses: Animals, clowns, and flying trapeze.

“That somethin’ you could do, Rir?”  

“Woof, you keep asking me this question today, Shuu… Since back then, I’m a bit afraid of heights, so no, I couldn’t.”  

“Makes sense.”

He patted her head with a somewhat satisfied look. He acted awfully cheerful today. Maybe he simply enjoyed his time here.

«On the trapeze are —, —, and —! Oh dear, what is Long-Heart doing up there?»

Mr. Mitsuo was among the troupe members who’d perform the trapeze trick. Was that alright, could he do that? The woman’s question made it sound like the whole thing was intentional. Or rather, that it was one of his appearances.

_Can Mr. Mitsuo do anything related to the circus? Though that’s probably why he acts both as troupe leader and clown._  

_Hm~, in Anazumu it seemed like his movements weren’t that sharp. I wonder if that was since he’d been there for hundreds of years._

The trapeze performance started. Two men with muscular arms and a graceful woman flew up and down through the air. They were clearly skilled.  

There was something like a trampoline underneath, so it wasn’t that nerve-wracking, but it was fun in a lively way.

«Oh, is Long-Heart giving it a try!?»

It looked like Mr. Mitsuo was finally taking on the challenge. He dangled in the air, holding on to the hand of a man who was hanging from the trapeze with his feet, then he moved to the feet of another person. He did well for some time, but then…

«Oh no~~, he fell!»

When he was at the point where he had to switch to the woman, the third member of the trapeze team, his hand slipped (likely on purpose) and fell towards the floor.

I could hear shouts of dismay and shock from the audience, but… he acrobatically turned his body in mid-air and landed on the trampoline. If you asked me, it was quite captivating.

“W-Woof, how scary! I got chills all over!”  

“Still, that was all planned, y’know?”  

“Woof~! That’s incredible.”

It looked like it was the right choice to go to the Love Long Circus for our triple date.

+++

# 582 – Curtain Call

The white tigers were done jumping through the sun-rings[1](https://re-library.com/translations/levelmaker/volume-19/chapter-582-curtain-call/#easy-footnote-bottom-1-117768). They had incredible intensity. Similar to when I saw a monster use magic, back when I still struggled against magic beasts.

«Thank you so much for watching the performance until the end!»

The circus’ theme song played in the background. It looked like this was the end of the show.

Well, it was fun. There had been parts with audience participation, but to some slight regret, they didn’t pick us. Incidentally, the man who showed me to Mr. Mitsuo’s office and then our group to the VIP seats had performed tricks on the trampoline.

One after the other, the troupe members came from behind the stage and waved at the audience.

«Once more, let me introduce all the members of the Long Love Circus Troupe who did their best during the performance! First, the members of the aerial acrobatics team-»

The aerial acrobatics team… the men and women making up the group who’d climbed up and down on the cloth at the beginning of the show linked hands and bowed to the audience. Following their example, the other performers did the same, repeatedly thanking the audience.

«Then, Long-Hart, our well-known clown!»

At the very end, Mr. Mitsuo was summoned by a sound effect and waved at the audience while performing three backflips in a row. How did he manage that without his wig or red nose falling off?

«And finally, me, —, your commentator!»

After the girl who’d done the commentary gave her name, all the troupe members gathered around Long-Heart. They then linked hands and gave a quick bow.

Together with a buzzing sound, a bright-red curtain embroidered in gold was lowered. It closed slowly… as if to evoke lingering feelings. Finally, it fully closed.  

The lights turned on, shattering the illusion.

«Thank you so much for visiting us today! When you leave, please make sure you don’t forget any of your belongings.»

At those words, most people gathered their luggage and rose from their seats.

“Oh, that was fun!”  

“It sure was!”  

“Woof, circuses are amazing… It was the first time I saw one, but it left such an impression…”  

“It did? Happy to hear that.”  

“Did you like it, Sakura?”  

“Yeah, it was incredible! I’m so happy I can see.”

While stating our impressions, we were about to get up, too.

«Attention, attention! Mr. Joujou Ayumu, the troupe leader has something to discuss with you, so would you kindly meet him in his office?»

But then we could hear this announcement. Well, it was lunchbreak now, so he probably had more time to talk.

“Sounds like I’m needed. I’ll be off.”  

“Alright. We’ll wait for you in the park.”

«Ah, an addition to the earlier announcement. My apologies, but could the group who came with Joujou Ayumu go with him to the troupe leader?»

So, he wanted to talk to all six of us. Did he plan to meet more people connected to Anazumu?

“Sounds like we’ll all go there,” Mika commented.  

“Ah-ha-ha, sorry for getting you caught up in this.”  

“It’s fine, Bro. Personally, I’d like to get a closer look at this man who was manipulated by an evil god.”  

“…True. I agree with Kanata,” Shuu added.

Thus, we gathered our luggage, left our seats, and made our way to the office I’d been shown to earlier.  

Before long, we arrived. After knocking and getting a reply, we entered.

“We’re here, so what is this about? The announcer said you have something to discuss.”  

“Ah, thank you for coming. Sorry for calling you here like that. Well, for now, please take a seat. Also, I apologize for still wearing make-up.”

The six of us sat down as he had asked us to. He took a seat somewhere he could face all of us.

“Alright. First, let me thank you. As Mr. Ayumu surely told you already, I am deeply grateful for returning to this world. Furthermore, I thank all of you for visiting my circus!”  

“It was incredible! It was my first time seeing a circus, but still…”  

“Oh, it brings me great joy to hear that.”

Mr. Mitsuo showed a truly glad smile when he heard Rir say that. While a good thing, it felt awfully weird to see a clown smile like this.

“The circus was really entertaining, and it brought me joy from the bottom of my heart… So, what is this matter you called us here for?”

In the end, Kanata, the most forceful among us, cut to the chase. It seemed as if he still harbored some suspicions.

“To be honest, I wanted to meet others who’ve been over there.”  

“I see, is that how it is?”

_K-Kanata, you look like you’re about to start a fight…_  

_I mean, it’s true that I explained that he used to be an enemy, but… ugh… if something happens, I’ll have to stop my brother._

Whether or not he noticed Kanata’s aggressive attitude, Mr. Mitsuo continued speaking.

#### Footnotes:

1. Not sure about this, the original is a bit weird. 日の輪くぐりが終わった (“finished going under/passing through/evading ring of sun”). I can only assume it’s the typical “big cat jumps through ring of fire”.[](https://re-library.com/translations/levelmaker/volume-19/chapter-582-curtain-call/#easy-footnote-1-117768)

# 583-1 – The Clown’s Future

This chapter isn’t a two-parter, the author simply messed up numbering them again.

---

“I… I am planning to continue living in this world as the leader of the circus troupe. Please rest assured that I won’t engage in any criminal acts.”

Usually, I’d expect Kanata to say something like “Talk is cheap” and further argue him down, but it looked like he deliberately didn’t do that. He merely kept silently looking at the clown.

“Well, I wasn’t involved in these matters, so it isn’t my place to judge… What about you, Bro?”  

“M-Me?”  

“I mean, you have to closest connection to this man, don’t you?”

He did have a point. I looked into Mr. Mitsuo’s eyes… To no surprise, the look he gave us was completely different from when he’d been Mephistophales.  

_I guess I should tell him my thoughts._

“Well, since I was the one who sent you back, it’s not my place to judge either. I had fun at the circus, and you did apologize to me.”

I took out the VIP card and moved my gaze to it. Lifetime VIP treatment… not that this made up for killing Mika and trying to do the same to me. Well, I couldn’t come up with any better apology he might’ve offered in his position, either.

“You did accept the death penalty in Anazumu, but I have no idea how many people you killed before that[1](https://re-library.com/translations/levelmaker/volume-19/chapter-583-1-the-clowns-future/#easy-footnote-bottom-1-117770). What you did to us and the people living in the Mephilad Kingdom was unforgivable, so I don’t plan to do so.”

The clown’s eyes darkened.

I wasn’t a saint who’d forgive that kind of thing. In the first place, doing that would mean I didn’t care about Mika dying. So, I would never forgive him. I wouldn’t, but-

“Make up for it by bringing smiles to many people on this side. And obviously don’t start committing crimes, otherwise…”

I shot Shuu a glance. He nodded.

“You should expect a visit from the police, soon. Furthermore, we’ll warn them to keep an eye of you while you’re in the area.”  

“Do you… have connections to the police or something[2](https://re-library.com/translations/levelmaker/volume-19/chapter-583-1-the-clowns-future/#easy-footnote-bottom-2-117770)?”  

“…More or less.”

When he heard that, Mr. Mitsuo looked relieved for some reason. I didn’t know what he was thinking, but maybe he was glad that someone would hold him back after he had caused so much trouble. I wasn’t as smart as my brother, so I couldn’t analyze his reactions.

“Erm, you’re Miss Mika, right?”  

“Y-Yes, that’s me.”  

“I am so sorry… for what happened in Anazumu…”  

“…I see.”

The clown addressed Mika after glancing at the clock, likely since he had to prepare for the next performance. She, who’d suffered the most among us because of him, seemed surprised by suddenly being spoken to, but managed to reply in a calm fashion.

“As Mr. Ayumu said, I will devote myself to making people smile in my circus.”

He was still in his clown make-up, so it was hard to see his expression as serious, but there was conviction in his voice.

I stood up. Kanata, reading the mood, also got up. The other four in our group followed our example.

“Understood. Do that, no matter what happens… We’ll come visit the circus again using these cards.”  

“…Of course, you’re always welcome.”  

“We’ll see ourselves out, then.”

We left the troupe leader’s office. Then, we vacated the premises the circus had rented and made our way to the park where we were planning to eat lunch.

“Bro, you told him to ‘bring smiles to people’…” Kanata commented with a grin after we sat down in a place with several sets of chairs and benches.  

“Wh-What about it? Isn’t it alright to say stuff like that once in a while?”  

“I mean… I just thought it sounded like something a light novel protagonist would say…”  

“Grr! Hmph!”

I impulsively puffed out my cheeks. Mika immediately pushed them together, causing them to deflate.

“Let’s eat already. That’s what we made the lunch boxes for!”  

“The three of you brought individual lunches, right? Should we spread them out on the table?”

The girls nodded at Kanata’s suggestion.

“Woof, that’s right! I made it for Shuu…”  

“I made mine for Ayumu…”  

“A-And I… for… uhm… Kanata.”

From the reaction, it looked like Mika had gotten Sakura to make it. Kanata was scratching his cheek with a happy expression.

The table was wide and there were ample chairs, so three people could sit on each side with room to spare, with us boys on one side and our respective partners opposite us.

“Look at that, isn’t that guy crazy?”  

“Right, he’s got a huge harem with him! Are they shooting a movie or something?”  

“Who knows… but it sure is insane to see a guy with that many cute girls.”

Those were the voices of young women passing by. The one who reacted most strongly to that wasn’t Shuu but Kanata.

“What, are they actually thinking I’m a girl…?”  

“Just give up. We’re siblings.”  

“Hmph!”

In an imitation to me, Kanata now puffed out his cheeks, and it was Sakura who caused them to deflate.

_…Huh, you’re asking what happened afterwards? We obviously started feeding each other. The whole group. I mean, that’s a forgone conclusion with this group. Also, the Karaage was super tasty._

---

**TL notes:**  

And that does it for the circus-arc, which wasn’t as bad as I expected. It remains to be seen what Jizou did to Mephistophales and if he’ll show again. The words back then certainly made it sound as if he’d fulfill the role of the guide.

I’m not counting everyone Samaeyl killed since I’m not convinced she wouldn’t have done that without him “manipulating” her.[](https://re-library.com/translations/levelmaker/volume-19/chapter-583-1-the-clowns-future/#easy-footnote-1-117770)

2. The original is 警戒の関係者 (“related person of vigilance”). Not sure if that’s supposed to be a vigilante or some expression you don’t find outside of Japan. I assume it’s meant more like “have contacts in the police”.[](https://re-library.com/translations/levelmaker/volume-19/chapter-583-1-the-clowns-future/#easy-footnote-2-117770)
