# Side Story 18 – Seinforce’s Date

“The wedding was wonderful.”

Ruin and Orgo, who’d personally attended the wedding between two fellow SSS-Rankers, where talking about that day.

“It turned out like that since Alim took care of it.”  

“You’re right… Say, Orgo. Should we just marry our partners already?”  

“About that… I feel like that’s something we should discuss individually with the girls.”  

“True…” Ruin nodded.

However, Orgo had a grim look on his face.

“I can’t help feeling that we’re forgetting something. What did we do since we started dating them?”  

“…Alim took us to level-up, and afterwards it was always all four of us when we spent time together.”

The two of them thought back over the past few months. Deep down, they were assailed by feelings of inadequacy.

“Hey, why don’t we go over these romance books again?”  

“Let’s do that.”

They went to the library and borrowed several books on romance. After flipping through them, a shock ran through them. The following was written on the page they had stopped at:

You managed to get together with a girl? The next step is to go on a date. This is essential. You completely forgot about that part, haven’t you? You probably haven’t even kissed and hugged her, have you? This is no laughing matter. You need to show affection to your partner!

The prince and his friend looked at each other. There was cold sweat on their faces. A book that had been written in the past managed to predict the current state of their relationships this accurately. Although they had hugged the girls in the way a close friend might do, it was never as someone of the opposite gender, let alone as lovers.

“A… a date. That’s right, a date! I completely forgot that part…”  

“Gods, it was always the four of us, so it totally slipped my mind! If this keeps going on, Lilo will start giving me the cold shoulder!”

The following was the panicked conclusion the two of them arrived at.

“”Let’s go on a date!””

They’d obviously take the girls on a date. Thus, they started making plans. Naturally, that was while consulting the romance guidebooks. And what they finally settled on was to:

Split up in two groups and each visit a date spot. The ultimate goal of this first date is to share a hug with the respective partner.

They had to strike while the iron was hot. They decided to ask their respective partners to go on a date right away.

_____  

___  

_

“Lilo, are you there?”  

“Hm, Ruin? Sure, come in.”

Ruin had come to Lilo’s room. He’d been there to chat often since they started dating. Still, most of those times, it had been all four of them.

“What brings you here today?”  

“Uhm, how about we go out somewhere next Sunday?”  

“The four of us?”  

“No, just the two of us… as in, on a date.”

She gave him a blank look. After going over what he had said in her mind, she gradually started to smile.

“Really?”  

“Yes, sorry for never asking until now. I couldn’t come up with anything.”  

“You finally~ asked. Eh-heh-heh, I’ve been waiting all that time, you know?”

The prince took a sigh of relief when she didn’t turn down his invitation to a first date and instead showed an expression of delight.

“I was afraid you’d get angry and turn me down after it took me so long.”  

“I’d never do that. It made me super happy! Did you already decide on a place?”  

“If there’s somewhere you’d like to go, we can pick that, otherwise I’ll look for a good place.”  

“Alright! Ruin, I love you, you know?”

His ears turned slightly red as he heard that. The one who said it also blushed as she smiled.

“Yes, I love you, too,” he replied.

_____  

___  

_

“H-Hey, uhm, are you there, Myuri?”  

“I am, please come in.”

Orgo was visiting Myuri’s room. The boy, shyer than his appearance would indicate, didn’t come to her room as often as Ruin to Lilo’s. It was at best once per week.

“What a nice surprise! What brings you here, Orgo? Did you come to chat?”  

“Well, there _is_ something I want to talk about.”

As she saw his thoughtful, serious expression, she was gripped by unease.

“Wh-What might that be…? Was it something I did? I barely changed how I acted since we started our relationship, so maybe-”  

“Th-That ain’t it! You’re jumping to conclusions.”

Orgo, in a rare case for him being able to sense where she was going with this, interrupted her. She wiped her moist eyes and smiled at him.

“I am happy to hear that. I was afraid I was inadequate as your girlfriend…”  

“I never thought that. It’s more that I’m the problem. I’m really sorry… The reason I came here today is to get out of this stalemate.”  

“Get out of this stalemate…?” Myuri inclined her head in confusion.

Orgo took a deep breath and then awkwardly continued.

“…Wh-Why don’t we go on a date? Just the two of us.”  

“Go on… a date?”  

“Exactly. A date.”

She forcefully got up from where she was sitting. Then, she jumped at him with an overjoyed expression.

“I would love to…! No matter what, let us go on a date!”  

“…Sure, let’s do that!”

While somewhat perplexed that he had managed to reach the ultimate goal before the date had even started, Orgo gently returned Myuri’s embrace. Unused to it, even though they were childhood friends, his face turned bright red.

---

**TL notes:**  

This will be an ongoing side story through the rest of the volume. I assume this is to sate the author’s craving for chapters with people flirting, since it looks like the rest of the volume will be more plot-centric, though that’s only judging from the chapter titles.

+++

# Side Story 19 – Seinforce’s Date – 2 (Orgo PoV)

“Orgo! Uhm… how do I look?”

It was the day of the date. Seinforce had split up into two groups – Orgo plus Myuri, and Ruin plus Lilo – and arranged to meet in different places inside the castle. The former two met in front of a conspicuous statue in the courtyard.

“Ah, well… I think you look nice.”  

“Really? Heh-heh, it gladdens me to hear that!”

What Orgo actually had wanted to use were words like “cute” or “lovely”, but instead a mere “nice” left his mouth. Contrasting with the girl’s happiness, the boy felt somewhat conflicted. Just as when he had confessed to her, he found himself unable to communicate his feeling clearly.

“Should we go, then?”  

“Yes.”

For now, he threw away any hesitation and started his first date with Myuri… or rather, his first date ever. The two of them left the white area.

Strictly speaking, both Orgo and Myuri were the children of nobles, so they were wearing fine garments. Although it was a different question whether such refined clothing suited the boy’s physique.

“So, where are you going to take me?”  

“Well… for now just come with me.”  

“Of course.”

He started walking. She followed, a step behind him. Orgo was aware of this habit of hers.

“Myuri.”  

“Yes, what might it be?”  

“Come, walk next to me.”  

“Eh…? Ah, of course!”

She herself, now realizing that she had fallen back into her habit of walking behind the others, hurriedly took a place next to the boy. Thus, they continued walking in that fashion. Still, she soon fell a step behind once more. While the boy noticed it, he decided not to mention it, knowing it was an old habit of hers.

“We’re here.”  

“Why…! A street filled with food-stalls!”  

“Exactly. I first thought we could go have fun and mess around somewhere… I mean, am I stupid? That probably would’ve ruined your clothes… so I thought of something else…”  

“Heh-heh, I do not mind. The important part is to have fun.”  

“I-I guess, anyway.”

They started walking down the street before coming to a stop in front of a stall.

“Oh my, it is one of those sandwich stalls!”  

“…At this point, these things are sold everywhere, huh?”  

“It is a simple dish invented by Alim; you merely put suitable ingredients between two slices of bread… It would appear that this stall sells sweet varieties.”  

“They’ve got lots more different kinds of those, now.”

They each quickly bought one and started eating it.

At this point, Orgo remembered something. In the romance guides they had perused while deciding on where to go for the date, there was an entry about “couples feeding each other during meals[1](https://re-library.com/translations/levelmaker/volume-19/side-story-19-seinforces-date-2-orgo-pov/#easy-footnote-bottom-1-117795).”

He stared at the sandwich he was holding; one with citrus fruits soaked in sweet sirup, with fresh cream forming a thin skin around it[2](https://re-library.com/translations/levelmaker/volume-19/side-story-19-seinforces-date-2-orgo-pov/#easy-footnote-bottom-2-117795). Then at Myuri, who was about take the second bite of hers with fresh cream and strawberries.

In truth, the two had been born almost at the same time and consequently spent much of their lives together, so there had been several times when they fed each other in the past. At those times, it hadn’t felt embarrassing… but now Orgo was more conscious of one fact. That it would serve as an indirect kiss.

“…Orgo, is something wrong?”  

“Eh… no, it’s just…”  

“Could it be that you would like to try some of mine? Heh-heh, I should have seen this coming. But only a single bite, if you would?” she conceded, as she held out her meal to him.

Finding no reason to refuse, he obediently took it.  

He swallowed and gathered his resolve, before taking a bite. It was sweet. Excessively sweet. Still, he couldn’t help feeling as if said sweetness wasn’t just due to the fruits and fresh cream.

“Was it that delicious? Might we swap, so I can try yours, too?”  

“Huh!? O-Oh, sure thing.”

Realizing how strange it would be not to offer his own sandwich after she had let him try hers, he readily handed her his meal. She accepted it with a smile and quickly took a bite. He watched the scene while carefully holding her strawberry sandwich.

“Yes, yours is also quite good! Here you go. Could I have mine back, please?”  

“Sure.”

Still somewhat out of it and captivated by her, he gave her sandwich back and took his own from her. Then, he gazed at the teeth mark she had left after taking a bite of it.

“…Is there something off about you today, Orgo?”  

“Wha-…!? You think so? Well… I guess. Maybe I’m having too much fun being on a date with you, Myuri. I’m definitely feeling excited.”  

“My heart has been racing all that time! Eh-heh-heh, it is a date, after all! I am also feeling excited!”

The boy’s mental defenses crumbled as she said this with a smile, blushing slightly.

After finishing their sandwiches (Orgo somehow managed after a bit of hesitation) they walked around the stalls, eating snacks as they went. They then left the street and, with Orgo in the lead, made their way to the next stop of their date. Myuri followed half a step behind him.

---

**TL notes:**  

There were some author’s comments, mentioning that it was originally planned to keep this to one date chapter for Orgo and Ruin each, but it blew up and is now three chapters each, which will be spread out over the rest of the volume.

#### Footnotes:

1. At this point, I think the author should consult one of those guides themselves. It’s the fifth couple we see, and there’s no variety at all.[](https://re-library.com/translations/levelmaker/volume-19/side-story-19-seinforces-date-2-orgo-pov/#easy-footnote-1-117795)

2. This may be wrong. It could be the sirup forming the thin skin, or it could have a completely different meaning that eludes me. Also, depending on the bread, this sounds like a mess waiting to happen.[](https://re-library.com/translations/levelmaker/volume-19/side-story-19-seinforces-date-2-orgo-pov/#easy-footnote-2-117795)

# Side Story 20 – Seinforce’s Date – 2 (Ruin PoV)

“…Alright.”

Ruin took a look at his pocket watch and nodded to himself. He was currently in front of Lilo’s room, the place they had chosen to meet up. He then knocked three times.

“Lilo, are you ready?”  

“Yes, I am. Come on in!”  

“Excuse me.”

The first thing he saw after entering the room was her. She was wearing one of the outfits she usually picked when they went out. _Cute_ was the first thought crossing his mind.

“We’re going on a date! I’m so excited, the heart in my chest keeps pounding.”  

“Yes, you’re right.”

Ruin had been educated as a prince and spent his days removed from sexual desires, but, as if compelled by his very nature as a man, he still turned his gaze to those exaggeratedly big twin-mounds. Most would likely agree that she had left him no choice after bringing attention to them herself with her words.

Assuming she’d think him uncouth for gazing at her chest like this, he hurriedly averted his eyes. It was also that he had become more aware of them, since they had moved from childhood friends to being a couple.

“Now, shall we go?”  

“…Let’s!”

He held out his hand.

Holding hands during the date… while this had been one of his goals, what he did right now happened unconsciously, being part of the conduct of a prince towards women, which had been ingrained in him.

Lilo was bewildered for a moment, but then carefully took his hand. Linking hands with him “as his girlfriend”; it filled her with both restlessness and elation as their hands entwined.

“Let’s walk around like this.”  

“Alright.”

The two of them left the castle. On their way, they stayed unaware of the many gazes of the maids and gardeners, Elle and Herrell, and the minister who watched them in secret. Seeing those two rather inexperienced youths brought smiles to the onlookers.

“So, you never told me anything. Where are we going?”  

“I was thinking of going to the Grand Mephilad Park to walk around and look at street-art and sculptures.”  

“A walk through the park? That sounds nice!”

Regarding the whole date affair as a serious matter, Ruin decided to go with a stylish approach. The place named “Grand Mephilad Park” was said to be one of the largest parks in the city. It was the site for numerous works of art and other things, so he decided on it for their date. And while it somewhat overlapped with Orgo’s idea, he was also considering eating snacks at the stalls scattered around the park.

“We’re here.”  

“So, what should we look at? How about the stone statues of past rulers?”  

“Right… yeah, let’s check those out.”

Still holding hands, the two of them made their way to their destination. There, statues of past kings were lined up. From incompetent rulers to shrewd politicians, there were all kinds of kings.

The only rulers enshrined in this manner were those who had passed already, so there was no statue of the current king. Furthermore, the man was still in his forties, so it likely would be several decades until the next addition.

“Hm~… no matter how often I see them, none of the past rulers’ faces look like yours, Ruin. Although they do have a similar air to them…”  

“Well, when my grandmother gave birth to my mother, she was said to look just like her. The three of us also seem to take more after our mother.”  

“You’ve got a point there. I also only got my father’s eyes and everything else from my mother.”

She let go of his hand and touched his face while showing a smile. He let it happen, although seemingly embarrassed by it.

“Should we go look at more?”  

“Alright… huh?”

Assuming he’d take it again, Lilo held out her hand. Only, he had done it unconsciously earlier and was now in a fluster.

“You want me to… take your hand?”  

“What? Haven’t we been holding hands all the time?”  

“Uh…”

Ruin racked his brains. Finally, he thought over the events between leaving the castle and arriving here. True enough, they had been holding hands all the time.

“S-Sorry. I did that completely unconsciously.”  

“You unconsciously took my hand? I guess we did walk around hand in hand when we were little, so maybe it’s a holdover from back then.”  

“R-Right, that’s probably it.”

He took her hand. The feeling of her skin was enough to cause him some elation.

“Your hands have gotten a lot bigger, Ruin, haven’t they?”  

“The same goes for yours, Lilo.”  

“Well, we grew up. Eh-heh-heh, in several places…”

He immediately understood the meaning behind her words and found his eyes being drawn to her chest. He instantly moved them away, looking at her face instead.

“What’s wrong?”  

“Ah… nothing. It’s just, you…”  

“What about me?”  

“… You’re just so cute.”  

“You… y-y-you think so? Thank you.”

She touched his hand for a moment, as if to caress it.

“So, should we go to the next spot?”  

“Yeah, let’s.”

The casually strolled towards their destination – a plaza filled with famous artworks – which would serve as their next date-spot.

+++

# 583-2 – Always

“Heh-heh-heh, Ayumu~.”

Mika was acting quite spoiled. We were currently in Anazumu and it was two days after we had watched the circus, at least from our perspective.

On Sunday, the day after our triple date, I’d have loved to get intimate with her, but it unfortunately proved impossible. There were appearances to consider, and we’d be in trouble if our parents walked in while we were in the middle of it. Making a stop at a love hotel under the pretext of taking a break while on a date… might have worked, though. Only, we’d both been tired, so all we’d done was lay around in Mika’s room, reading manga and playing video games.

“Ayumu! I love~ you!”  

“Eh-heh-heh, me too.”

_Ah, bliss._

Afternoon coffee… or rather, café au lait plus a good amount of cookies. This and my beloved childhood friend. Could there be nicer afternoon? It was so laid-back.  

In this world, we generally didn’t do any work at the beginning of the week. Thus, we could spend our time relaxing.

“Hey, Ayumu.”  

“Hm, what is it?”  

“Today… how about we do it?” she asked with her head cocked, like a kitten begging for attention.

That was against the rules. Even though her mere presence was enough to beguile men, she now struck a cute pose that left even me, her childhood friend for 15 years turned fiancé, feeling dizzy.

“Hm, alright.”  

“Eh-heh-heh… on Earth, we can’t share a bed naked and take it all the way.”  

“D-Don’t forget that even here, Kanata and the others are living under the same roof.”  

“That’s fine. This place is completely soundproofed.”

She brought her mouth closer, which I welcomed with my own. Kissing was still some rite of passage. Though just a short few months ago, this alone would’ve been enough to make my heart jump out of my throat.

_Oh, I can taste the café au lait. Both slightly bitter and sweet._

“Phew, alright then. Let’s move to the bed.”

Ever since her birthday, being picked up in a princess carry always made Mika quite happy. For that reason, I was about to do just that and bring her to the bed, but…

“Ah, wait a moment,” she stopped me.  

“What’s wrong?”  

“Can’t we switch things up a bit?”  

“Hm? Sure, I guess.”

When she made such a suggestion, we usually changed either the location or what we were wearing. It was part of keeping things interesting and happened about once every five times we did it.

“Also, there’s something I wanted to ask; which one do you prefer, how I am here or on Earth?”  

“What!?”

I didn’t expect that at all. Where was she going with that? Either way, the answer was clear.

“I love both versions of you from the bottom-”  

“I knew you’d say that. That wasn’t how I meant it. Uhm… it’s a question of physique.”

She was fidgeting, likely since saying it out loud felt embarrassing to her. It looked cute. In any case, what did she mean by physique?

“W-We can change the color of our hair as we want, right? On Earth, you say that you love my pretty, black hair, and here you call it a gem-like emerald-green. Still, you’re the only one who has the power to change age and physical shape, aren’t you?”

She had a point. She was likely wondering whether I preferred her 13- or 16-year-old version. And depending on my answer, she’d want me to use something created with Item Master to change our appearances to those on Earth for today… more or less.

“So tell me, would you rather have this flat version of me that looks like a seventh grader, or the busty 16-year-old me?”

In other words, this was about whether I preferred her breasts large or small (though still comparatively big for her age).

I never had such a preference. I mean, I owned adult magazines, but I never picked those with especially busty girls. Unlike Shuu.

Going even further, I didn’t have any preference when it came to figure, butt, or legs. Frankly speaking, I liked her for who she was. Whether she had big or small breasts didn’t matter to me. Still, I was faced with a choice now.

_Think, me. I’ve seen her naked on both sides… so which one do I like more…_

“In that case, should we use items to make us look like we do on Earth?”  

“Yeah! Eh-heh-heh, in any case, I’m happy to hear that. I’d have been troubled if you’d chosen my less-developed form, even given the option of the mature one.”

That was certainly true. If I had done that, it would paint me a pedophile.  

_Huh? Am I one already since I’ve done it with her several times on this side while she looked like this? No, there’s a difference._

“So, are you going to create an item? I’ll be going to the bedroom ahead of you today.”  

“Alright!”

I quickly made the item. Well, it was pretty much instantaneously.  

I threw the completed device, which was shaped like a ball, into our bedroom. With this, we’d look like we did on Earth for some time.

“…Now then, come to me!” Mika called in a tempting voice.  

“…Yes!”

She was already fully prepared, so I crawled next to her into the bed.

“Eh-heh-heh… You can do whatever you want with me.”  

“In that case, I’ll take you up on that-”

It happened the moment I extended my hand towards her chest.

⟦Alim, Mika! It is Us, Rama[1](https://re-library.com/translations/levelmaker/volume-19/chapter-583-2-always/#easy-footnote-bottom-1-117799)! We discovered somewhat concerning literature! Are you busy right now?⟧

# 584 – Another Call

“…”  

“…”

Mika and I fell silent as we looked at each other.  

_No way… this can’t be happening. How many times does this make? Is he psychic and aiming for these moments? Or has he installed hidden cameras here?_

⟦Are you there, Alim, Mika?⟧  

⟦…Sorry, we’re in the middle of something right now.⟧  

⟦N-No need to get angry. Our apologies for contacting you at a bad time.⟧  

⟦…Uhm, could you call us back tomorrow?⟧  

⟦Call you back… you say? Oh, well, We shall do so. We are not in a hurry.⟧

The king meekly cut off the message. That ruler who took Kanata and Sakura in his care might’ve summoned them by force, at least from what he told me.  

King Mephilad and King Rama weren’t like that, they were decent people. Only, they were completely~ unable to read the room.

_Hmph._

“Ayumu, you’re puffing out your cheeks again, you know?”  

“…Hah. Since when!?”  

“Did that ruin the mood for you? We could pick it up again at a later time.”

_Pick it up a later time… huh. No, that won’t work. I’ll be even less in the mood then._

“No, let’s go back to it right away.”  

“That’s the spirit! I love you.”

She hugged me. Neither of us was wearing anything, so her large breasts were…  

In any case, we started again from our kiss.

__________  

_____  

__

⟦So, what is this important matter you called for yesterday, Your Majesty?⟧

It was the next day. I was talking with King Rama, who’d contacted us again as previously agreed upon.

On another note, it looked like Mika had enjoyed it more than usual yesterday, so she’d likely want us to do it in our older appearances again. Well, it wasn’t like I had any objections. I had been attracted to her for a long time, so I was more used to see her in her Earth appearance… which somehow made things a lot more exciting.

⟦Alim, did you hear what We just said?⟧  

⟦N-No, my apologies.⟧  

⟦Hrm. We shall say it again.⟧

According to what King Rama kindly explained a second time, his palace librarian discovered the diary of a previous king when he organized the archives. Assuming it might give them some insight into the past, King Rama and the librarian read this diary of the former’s great-grandfather[1](https://re-library.com/translations/levelmaker/volume-19/chapter-584-another-call/#easy-footnote-bottom-1-117927) and learned something extraordinary.

⟦Alim, you might remember that We briefly told you about Our country’s history.⟧  

⟦You did. So, what was it about…?⟧  

⟦The guide. Our great-grandfather nominated a guide. Even though there is no mention of a guide appearing in recent literature…⟧

True enough, I remembered the king mentioning that no guide had been designated in a long time. And despite that, he now learned that his very great-grandfather had nominated one.

⟦Is the account reliable?⟧  

⟦Yes, the man was said to be sincere… although there also are some mischievous parts in the diary. More importantly, We would like to ask you for a favor, Alim.⟧

_A favor? What might that be?_

⟦What do you need me for, Your Majesty?⟧  

⟦Well, the reason We contacted you wasn’t solely because you’re the hero… The diary is old and weathered, so parts of some pages have become illegible. We would ask you to restore it.⟧  

⟦Oh, something like that should be no problem for me!⟧

_That’s what he’s after? Restoring some old documents…? Not exactly my usual work._

⟦Understood. In that case, We shall send an envoy with it right away.⟧  

⟦Oh, no need for that. We’ll come to you.⟧  

⟦Aren’t you busy? From Our knowledge, you should have work tomorrow.⟧  

⟦Uhm, well…⟧

_How does he know what? That’s a bit worrying… oh, whatever._  

_As a fan, he probably has a handle on when our photoshoots and such are._

⟦We can go wherever we want instantly thanks to my items. Paying you a visit right away and returning on the same day should be easy enough.⟧  

⟦I-I see! Does that mean you and Mika will visit Our country?⟧  

⟦It does… I guess?⟧

I gave Mika, who’d just been listening, a glance. The king’s reply had sounded strangely excited. Was he that happy about me paying him a visit?

⟦In any case, We take it you will be visiting Us, then. We shall be awaiting you.⟧  

⟦Indeed, it will take about ten minutes.⟧  

⟦T-Ten minutes!? You will be here that soon?⟧  

⟦Yes, it’s possible.⟧

At least if we were able to borrow Kanata’s power[2](https://re-library.com/translations/levelmaker/volume-19/chapter-584-another-call/#easy-footnote-bottom-2-117927). Well, I didn’t expect him to refuse, as long as we explained the situation to him.

And while we were there, it might be a good idea for me to treat this like a vacation in another country with Mika.

⟦So, you will be visiting Us right now?⟧  

⟦Yes, we will.⟧

Mika and I ended the connection with King Rama.

_Now._

“Let’s go ask Kanata whether he’ll teleport us.”  

“Hm, alright.”

# 585 – To the Bufura Kingdom!

“That’s about it, could you do that for us, Kanata?”  

“Sure thing.”

After explaining the situation to my brother, who’d apparently been playing chess with Sakura, he agreed right away.  

_How nice of him… makes me proud of him as his older sibling._

“Just send me a message once you need me to pick you up again… But if it gets later than 11 pm, please stay the night there and contact me after 5 am.”  

“Sounds like someone’s planning to snuggle tonight with my little sister.”  

“…Yes, you’re correct with that assumption, Mika-nee. You wouldn’t want to wake her up, would you?”

After smoothly parrying Mika’s verbal jab, he motioned for us to get closer. Mika and I obviously took that as our cue to hug each other.

“I’ll be sending you off, then.”  

“”Alright.””

The moment we gave our reply, our surroundings changed. No matter how often you experienced it, teleportation was incredible. The change in scenery signified that we had arrived in the Bufura Kingdom’s capital.

We were in a backstreet alley, which Kanata had likely picked so we wouldn’t cause a fuss. We were already in disguise, so we should be able to leave the alley and walk through town confidently.

“The hell!? When did these brats get here!?”

A man who could only be described as “thuggish” had appeared behind us.

Right, unlike in the Mephilad Kingdom, where we could conveniently throw all the criminals into jail during that temporary case of mass-death, the backstreets in the Bufura Kingdom weren’t safe. That part slipped my mind. Even disguised, Mika and I looked like pretty girls.

_Oh, no, we’re in danger!_

“Man, look at ’em more closely. They’re super pretty.”  

“Oh-ho, ain’t that the truth.”

Even more men closed in. Including Mika and me, there were six people in the narrow alley. It was rather suffocating.

“Guess we gotta catch ’em and sell ’em off.”  

“Nah, man, let’s use ’em first. With how pretty they are, going a few rounds with us probably won’t decrease their value.”  

“Huh… I mean to start with, they’re wearin’ some pricey stuff.”

They kept staring at us. It might’ve just been for form’s sake, but I stepped in front to protect Mika. Well, it didn’t look as if she was concerned about such a small matter.

“Well then… this’ll hurt a bit, but you gotta put up with that.”

The man who’d discovered us at the beginning pulled out a knife. It made me wonder if these guys were complete idiots, after going back and forth about our “value”.

“Man, catch ’em with your hands! They’ll be worth less if they have wounds.”  

“Oops, my bad.” He put away the knife.

This situation reminded me of when Uruto came to my rescue. A lot had changed since back then. I gave an internal chuckle.

“Oy, what’s with the grin?”  

“Oops, my bad.”

Apparently, my amusement had been noticed.

“Gah… whatever. Just catch ’em!”

The man in front came towards us and tried to put his arms around Mika and me. I took advantage of that to get close and personal to him to deliver a kick that would be just shy of killing him. He was blown away in a nice, straight line.

“…Wha-?”

From our attackers’ perspective, it must’ve looked as if it happened in an instant. They seemed stunned as their friend (or accomplice) flew away.

“H-Huh~!? She sent him flyin’!?”  

“That brat kicked a large adult away… don’t tell me she got high stats!?”  

“You might be right, man! We gotta bolt!”

Instead of going after us, they quickly turned to flee. It was a much smarter course of action than to assume they were mistaken and doubling down on the assault.

“It’s been a long time since something like this happened.”  

“It might’ve gone differently if we weren’t in disguise,” Mika replied.

We immediately left the backstreet alley. For the public order to be this bad so close to the main street… I should tell King Rama to do something about that later. Maybe I could create devices to improve public safety and hand those to them.

“Alright, let’s go!”  

“Yeah!”

We held hands. I was thinking of parading through town, as if on a date.  

I had heard that this place was famous for spices, and they got more sunlight, so many people showed a tan. The houses were also typical for that kind of climate.

“Somehow, it feels like we’re in India.”  

“I get what you mean.”

This wasn’t Earth, but the scenery resembled the pictures of India you often saw on TV. It made me want to eat curry rice.

Well, rice hadn’t been a thing in this world until I introduced it, and they didn’t have curry either[1](https://re-library.com/translations/levelmaker/volume-19/chapter-585-to-the-bufura-kingdom/#easy-footnote-bottom-1-118162). Though maybe they had something like naan.

“Here we are. King Rama’s palace.”  

“Right.”

At the very center, towering over everything else, stood a palace with a round roof.  

_Huh, it’s quite sparkly. Different from the Mephilad Kingdom’s western-style castle._

We soon arrived at its gates.  

_Now to get inside._

1. You’d think with an otherworlder every decade or so on average, someone would’ve introduced it at this point.[](https://re-library.com/translations/levelmaker/volume-19/chapter-585-to-the-bufura-kingdom/#easy-footnote-1-118162)

# 586 – Bufura Palace

“What brings you girls here? You’re not from this country, are you? Did you come here to sight-see?”

The gate guards had stopped us. In Mephilad, we lived close to the castle and going in and out was easy on account of everyone knowing us. Though right now, we were in disguise, so it wasn’t that simple.

“Ah, no, we have been invited by King Rama.”  

“Huh? You were invited by His Majesty…? It is true that he announced an invitation for Alim and Mika today, but…”  

“It might be faster if we showed you our adventurer cards.”  

“You look so young, but you have adventurer cards… no way!?”

At that point, the guard seemed to understand and could no longer hide his shock. Mika and I showed him our cards.

“Oh~, I s-s-see that you are Lady Alim Nariwei and Lady Mika Magarigi!!”  

“…Don’t you need to take the cards to inspect them more closely?”  

“S-Someone like me isn’t fit to touch your cards! Now, please go on through!”

The other guard who hadn’t talked helped open the gates with a somewhat excited expression.

“Is it alright if we remove the disguise now?”  

“O-Of course! Even should someone make their way inside, we shall make sure that you won’t be harmed, My Ladies! Please go ahead and undo your disguises!”  

“Thank you.”

Mika and I turned off the disguise and then walked through the gate into the palace grounds. The guards kept staring after us, though that was something we were used to.

As we traipsed through the palace gardens, an old man with dark skin and a white moustache appeared in front of us and have us a deep bow.

“Lady Alim Nariwei and Lady Mika Magarigi, I presume? We welcome you. I shall show you the way.”  

“Nice to meet you!” I replied.  

“It’s a pleasure to make your acquaintance!” Mika said.  

“L-Likewise!”

The old man’s eyes sparkled in apparent delight. It instantly ruined his dignified gentlemanly image.

“This might sound overly self-conscious, but it feels like we have an awful lot of fans in this country,” I mused, having sensed that this old gentleman was also one of said fans. “Is there a reason for that?”

As a matter of fact, while we’d walked through the city here, I’d seen enough posters of me to fill the Mephilad royal capital. It was one thing over there, seeing that was where I had become famous, but this place was far away.

“You are already acquainted with our king, aren’t you? As you no doubt learned, he is quite the fanatical fan of the two of you. Moreover, this started before you were declared the hero, Lady Alim.”

_Huh, he was my fan even before I became the hero? I guess I should cherish this kind of devotion. Well, that still doesn’t mean I’ll go out with him or marry him._

“To be honest, it unsettled everyone at the beginning. For our ruler to be infatuated by some girl we knew nothing about… However, once posters and well-made realistic depictions of you started to circulate in our country, people changed their minds…”

_I see, so at the start, they were suspicious of me, but once they saw my face, they were spellbound. The usual pattern._

“In other words, most people in this country have become your zealous fans. Including me.”  

“Does that mean you want us to sign something?”  

“Oh, are you talking about writing your name on an article to increase its value…? You don’t mind? It doesn’t have to be obvious…”  

“Well, think of it more like something to remember our encounter. Is that fine for you?”  

“Of course.”

On that note, it went without saying that the concept of signing things was also something I introduced.

The old gentleman happily spread out a poster. The moment he did, Mika and I put our signatures on it in a split second.

“Could you please… huh?”  

“We have already signed it.”  

“Are you happy with it like this?”  

“I shall keep it as a family heirloom.” The old man gave us another deep bow.

While thinking that a simple signature wouldn’t make something an heirloom, I appraised it and learned that it was now treasure grade. The mere act of signing it was enough to elevate its value that much. That was worrying.

“Allow me to show you the way, then.”  

“We are in your care.”

We followed our gentlemanly fan through the gardens into the palace. There, we were welcomed by a crowd of bowing maids and servants. Somehow, this gave me a feeling of déjà vu. Though hearing the squeals and excited voices didn’t feel bad.

“What do you think of the palace?” the old man asked us.  

“Somehow it feels very Arabian!”  

“Arabi…? Might that be some new dish?”

That word obviously didn’t make any sense to the people here. Though the maids also were wearing colorful red and yellow outfits made of fluttering fabric.

“Welcome and thank you for coming, Alim, Mika!”

Shortly later, we saw King Rama excitedly descend a staircase. My senior fan welcomed us with a radiant smile.

“Thank you for having us.”  

“We wouldn’t mind if you stayed here permanently.”  

“No, thank you.”  

“…A pity.”

There was no need to look _that_ dejected! I probably should’ve chosen my words more carefully.

# 587 – The Diary of King Rama’s Great-Grandfather

“So, could you show us this diary of your ancestor right away?”  

“Yes, it is currently in the palace archives. Let’s go.”

Mika and I followed his lead. It looked like our gentlemanly fan, who’d shown us the way earlier, and the other servants would also join us.

In the end, the man was a king, so there were likely always several attendants with him when he walked through the palace. Still, King Mephilad wasn’t like that… he had at most two to three people with him.

“Hrm, why are you all following Us? You are aware that Alim and Mika are guests and that We are planning to show them something! Go back to your work!”

At the king’s words, most of the servants reluctantly left, with the only ones remaining being the old gentleman, the king’s personal bodyguard Hanuman, whom we’d met before, and a scholar who was likely charged with studying the diary.

“Our apologies for this disgraceful display.”  

“N-Not at all, Your Majesty.”  

“Well, that’s how it is, you are awfully famous in Our country, Alim… We’ve arrived.”

The king came to a stop in front of a door. This was likely either the archive or the library.

In the case of the Mephilad Kingdom, the library wasn’t in the castle itself but a nearby building. In exchange, the castle itself only had an archive with a small selection of books. Karua had once complained to us that it was “such a bother to leave the castle whenever one wants to read a book.” Well, it only took a few minutes to get there from the castle.

“Hrm, where did We put it again… Ah, there!”

Where he was pointing, a thick, important-looking book was lying on a desk. This was probably the diary.

“As We mentioned via message, it is awfully weathered. The most crucial parts – what happened after the nomination of the guide – are illegible… It was Our blunder that it was left here for so long without anyone noticing its importance.”

So, they found some literature that might have a big historical significance, only for it to be weathered and falling apart. An all too familiar story.

On Earth, there was advanced restoration technology, with research institutes specialized on it, like the one investigating Kanata’s brain and Sakura’s eyes… Using methods I didn’t exactly know much about, they managed to completely restore ancient documents, often causing major changes to the historical record. Such changes obviously also included things like schoolbooks. That was the reason the ones from my parents’ generation were quite different from ours[1](https://re-library.com/translations/levelmaker/volume-19/chapter-587-the-diary-of-king-ramas-great-grandfather/#easy-footnote-bottom-1-118166).

Doing something like that would now be my job.  

_Heh-heh, this is kinda fun._

“Do you want me to only restore this book?”  

“Let Us think… Now that you bring it up, since you are here already, could We ask you to fix some other books, too? You there, I assume there are numerous historically important tomes that suffered wear and tear! Inform the librarians right away and have them bring those here! Hanuman, go and get some soldiers to help. These tomes are heavy.”  

“As you wish, My King.”

The way he was able to quickly hand down orders gave him a cool and aloof air. Although I knew that he was like an idol-obsessed otaku at his core.

“Well, Our apologies for that. Your compensation will be per book in that case.”  

“I-It’s no problem. I didn’t come here expecting to be paid to begin with.”

King Rama gave me a blank look when he heard my reply.

“What do you mean?”  

“To be blunt, doing this helps me kill time.”  

“We see. Even so, We must compensate you for this.”

Surprisingly enough, he wouldn’t back down. Well, if he was so insistent on paying me, then I wouldn’t refuse.

“Understood. Let’s restore the diary first, then.”  

“Please do.”

I put on gloves before picking up the book. It certainly was in a poor state. Still, all it took was to sprinkle some “Amrita for Items” on it and…

“Here you go, it should be back in the state it was when something was last written in it.”  

“That was all?”  

“Yes.”

Even I had to say that this restoration substance was awfully convenient. Though I didn’t use it often.

“In that case… hrm.”

The king picked up the diary and intently looked at its front and back cover. Then, he rifled through the pages. He nodded in apparent satisfaction.

“It has been fully restored. Marvelous.”

I gave a giggle while looking smug.  

_Not good, now he’s staring at me. I mustn’t act this flirtatiously in front of fans. It’s hard to keep calm when people stare like this._

“I brought some books to start with.”

The scholar who’d come with us earlier was back, carrying several dilapidated tomes. Just from looking at them, I could tell that they were several hundreds of years old.

“I see, you brought those first. They are historically valuable accounts We might gain ample information from, were they to be restored. But We were lacking the means for that, so We merely kept them in storage for the time being. Can you fix them, Alim?”  

“Piece of cake.”

I poured the same restoration fluid from earlier over the three books. In front of our eyes, they rapidly reverted to the state they had been when they were new.

“Oh… how wonderful!”  

“My King! Lady Alim! We brought more books!”  

“Hrm, those are also historical records! Ha-ha-ha, We might end up advancing our historical studies at once in a fell swoop!”

It looked like the librarians were back, carrying tons of books.  

_Alright, let’s fix all of those!_

#### Footnotes:

1. I feel like that’s a bad example since a) most changes to schoolbooks happen due to advancements in education, and b) Japan is notorious for “forgetting” much of the country’s less glorious recent history
