# 588 – Book Restoration

“Phew… that takes care of all of them!”

There was a veritable mountain of books. Looking at them now, it seemed incredible that I had fixed all of them. Likely excited after seeing some tomes restored, the librarians and soldiers who’d come to help only quickened their pace, so we ended up with this huge amount.

“This far exceeds the number of books We were planning to ask you to restore…” the king mused.  

“O-Our apologies. We thought we’d ask her to fix all of them, since we had the opportunity,” a librarian replied timidly. “Mostly since it appeared that the process of restoring them didn’t take all that long.”  

“You fool! What we witnessed wasn’t the part that took the most time. She had to prepare all this liquid before coming here. Am I assuming correctly?”  

“Y-Yes, this is correct.”

These people likely knew that I could produce items in a limitless quantity. Maybe they were just trying to show off in front of me, given they were my fans. Oh, whatever.

“Still, this really was a great help. Every last one of them looks brand new.”  

“Even the books that were old and tattered when we obtained them are now pristine.”  

“Eh-heh-heh.”

It felt good to somehow contribute to the study of history, as if I was part of their cycle.

“We’re thinking of reopening the investigation of the diary right away!” the scholar said.  

“Oh, that reminds me!”

This might be perceived as meddling, but I did have a proposal for them. Or rather, I had the perfect item for their research. It was something I’d been relying on even before I reached my current strength. Well, I still did for studying.

“Is something wrong, Alim?”  

“Do you need tools for speed-reading? I could lend them to you!”  

“We already have seven articles that allow you to read at ten times the normal speed, so We should be good.”  

“Well, the ones I’m talking about are-”

I’d since made several improvements to my speed-reading glasses.

First, you could freely adjust the reading speed from normal up to a thousandfold increase. Furthermore, they automatically interpreted and understood the contents of books and would tell the user of important commonalities when reading other books using the same pair of glasses. At this point, they were an exceptional tool.

It was incredible that they could do all this at legend grade.

“Hah… How were you even able to make something like that, Alim…? In that case, We would like to borrow several pairs. We assume that you can create more of them, is that correct?”  

“Of course!”  

“If possible, We would take a pair that you used previously, Alim… No, don’t look at Us like that! It was a joke!”

In any case, I let them borrow five of the improved speed-reading glasses.

“This should help Our investigation… All of you, We are counting on you.”  

“Yes!”  

“Thank you for your hard work, soldiers and librarians. You may return to your posts… You do have work to do, don’t you…? Will you leave Us already?!”

Contrasting with those who left immediately to work on their research, the other librarians and soldiers kept looking at me with a hint of regret. Mika and I decided to work together to get them back to their work.

“Everyone!”  

“Would you please…”  

“”…go back to your work?””

We winked while holding hands.  

_Ah, Mika’s so cute I might faint._

“Hah, we’re going~…”  

“Whatever you shay… eh-heh-heh…”

It looked as if they had sudden bouts of weakness, as they made their way back to their workplace with entranced expressions. We did it!

“So, King Rama, is there anything else you need from-”  

“Heh-heh-heh-heh-heh-heh-heh-heh…”

Oh, no, I completely forgot that our biggest fan was still here. He stood there looking happy with his mouth standing open and blood dripping from his nose. It was unfortunate to see him in such a sorry state, which how handsome he normally looked… It reminded me of a certain someone from Earth. Another déjà vu.

_________  

_____  

__

“Our apologies, the two of you looked simply so cute, We ended up losing Our composure.”  

“Ha-ha-ha.”

This went way beyond “losing your composure”! Even after ten minutes, he hadn’t come back to his senses. Our charm was a scary thing.

“In any case, that should do it for this matter.”  

“We have work tomorrow, so we’ll be going home, Your Majesty.”  

“When we visit again, we’ll make proper time, so Alim and I can go on a date,” Mika added.  

“We see, feel free to do so.”

There was a smack… or rather, a heavy thump as the king placed a pile of large gold coins onto the parlor’s table. This was probably my pay.

“Once more, you have Our thanks.”  

“Of course! This should be it for us.”  

“Once We have the results of the investigation, We’ll contact you. With the seals of several evil gods breaking in succession, it likely would be better for you to stay informed.”  

“We won’t say no, in that case.”

_I guess all that remains is to contact Kanata to bring us back. Hang on, I’m forgetting something… Right, that matter about the backstreet alley. Not good, I should keep better track of these things._

“My apologies, but there is another matter we wanted to talk to you about.”  

“Hrm, what might that be?”  

“It concerns this country’s public safety…”  

“Ah, that. We presume you perceived it as poor.”

It sounded like the king was aware of the issue.

“Yes. We were targeted by some ruffians… although we were in disguise at that point.”  

“What? Do you remember their faces? We shall capture them right away and put them to death!”  

“Th-That’s going a bit far. Was that another joke, Your Majesty?”  

“…I was serious. This country’s biggest issues are the caste system and poor public safety. If only there was something we could do.”

_Now, how far should I go to help with this?_

+++

# 589 – According to Literature

“Why is the public safety so bad in the first place?” I asked.  

“We know the reason for that. It’s because of the caste system.”

That was probably correct. Those who were sick of the system and chose a life of crime, or those who had no choice since they lived in poverty due to their low social standing… there must’ve been many people like that.

“In the end, something has to be done to change that.”  

“…We agree. It absolutely needs to happen during Our generation,” the king firmly declared. “Our subjects might be the ones to cause trouble… but We are the one who needs to do something about it.”

He was an SSS-Rank adventurer, strong enough to possess a Master skill, but he was still trying to achieve more. It was commendable, even considering his obsession with me. I had to give respect where it was due.

_In that case, I can’t do anything strange to help. He himself declared that he would do something, so it isn’t my place to butt in._

“I see, uhm… please do whatever you can, Your Majesty!”

My genius younger brother surely would’ve known something more appropriate to tell him, but I wasn’t that gifted, so that was all I came up with.

“Heh-heh, if you, Alim, tell Us to do whatever We can, then that’s exactly what We’ll do! Watch Us, as We get rid of discrimination like that SSS-Rank hero!” he proclaimed, full of energy.

_Yep, he can look cool when he puts his mind to it._  

_Anyway, we should go home._

“With that matter being settled, too, we’ll be on our way.”  

“Do you have work tomorrow?”  

“Yes, we have.”

We would be interviewed for an article.

“It must be tough. You seem busier than any other SSS-Ranker.”  

“It’s not that bad. It has been a while since we did actual adventurer work.”  

“We see. Your main occupation has changed towards modeling. Still, you seem rather busy.”  

“It’s true, that’s why we don’t act as adventurers unless a wild SSS-Rank magic beast were to appear… or something on that level.”  

“That is one way to go about it.”

_Well… to be blunt, I’m more of a crafter/idol than an adventurer at this point. Anyway, time to be off…_

“W-W-W-We discovered something astounding, Your Majesty!”  

“Huh, what is it!?”

The scholar who’d left just earlier had returned, looking rather agitated. For him to be back so soon… he must’ve picked the 1000-times reading speed setting.

“It is about the weapon used to seal the evil god! Just like the Hero’s Sword of the Mephilad Kingdom and Yggdrasil’s ‘Gungnir[1](https://re-library.com/translations/levelmaker/volume-19/chapter-589-according-to-literature/#easy-footnote-bottom-1-118573)‘, our country used to have a weapon effective against the evil god!”  

“What… is that true!?”

_Huh, isn’t that backwards? Shouldn’t they know about that?_

“Didn’t you know about that…?”  

“Well, somewhat. It is said that the weapon disappeared the moment the evil god was destroyed. It is quite an old story, so technically We knew about it, but-”  

“We had no knowledge about what kind of weapon it was! Thanks to your help, Lady Alim, we now do.”

_That’s great._

In the end, it took a lot to seal evil gods in the first place. When we sealed Surtr, he said that he wouldn’t be able to break out, so if it had ended in this manner… maybe the world would’ve completely forgotten about it 1000 years from now.

_No, 1000 years would be too short. There are still tons of books left from that time. In that case, isn’t it weird that there are so few books left mentioning the weapon that sealed the evil god[2](https://re-library.com/translations/levelmaker/volume-19/chapter-589-according-to-literature/#easy-footnote-bottom-2-118573)? Well, not my place to worry that much about it. If anything happens, all we need to do is take care of the evil god._

“So, what kind of weapon is it?” the king asked.  

“A vajra, Your Majesty.”  

“A vajra?”  

“Indeed, I’ll show you the part in the diary right away.”

I didn’t know what to make of the illustration the scholar showed us. At best, it reminded me of a rather ornate dumbbell[3](https://re-library.com/translations/levelmaker/volume-19/chapter-589-according-to-literature/#easy-footnote-bottom-3-118573).

“It seems to work similar to a staff or wand.”  

“A staff? This thing? It’s true that there are those who use instruments and such as magical foci, though…”  

“Well, it might be part of that category.”

The SSS-Ranker Heimdal and Gog, who was part of Lahand’s party, used weapons like that. Swords, spears… and then bows and staves seemed obvious, but this thing looked unusual.

“…That’s right, you were able to craft the Hero’s Sword, Alim, weren’t you? Would you be able to recreate this weapon?” the king asked.  

“I could, but… what for?”  

“Evil gods are frightening beings… It would be just in case. We shall pay you however much you wish, so can’t you craft it for Us!? No pressure, it could be whenever you have time.”

_This went in a strange way. Looks like I’ll end up recreating this so-called vajra._

“Uhm… it would be at least one week from now. Would that be alright with you, Your Majesty?”  

“Yes, We don’t mind if it takes some time.”

_So, I’ll really make it?_  

_Well, it is a direct request, so I’ll go about making it earnestly, but surely just by crafting the weapon, the evil god won’t come back to life, right?_

#### Footnotes:

1. The original is エクスカリバー (“Excalibur”). While I can’t discount the possibility of Alim having forgotten the name and thus not calling out the mistake, I assume it’s an error.[](https://re-library.com/translations/levelmaker/volume-19/chapter-589-according-to-literature/#easy-footnote-1-118573)

2. I can think of several reasons for this knowledge getting lost, especially if it poses some kind of danger.[](https://re-library.com/translations/levelmaker/volume-19/chapter-589-according-to-literature/#easy-footnote-2-118573)

3. The [vajra](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Vajra) is a ritual weapon from Hinduism, Buddhism, and Jainism. Alim’s description is pretty accurate.[](https://re-library.com/translations/levelmaker/volume-19/chapter-589-according-to-literature/#easy-footnote-3-118573)

+++

# Side Story 21 – Seinforce’s Date – 3 (Orgo PoV)

“This place is nice, no matter how often we come here,” Orgo muttered.

Myuri was looking at him.

“We have come here even since we were little. Do you remember those times?”  

“Yes, I remember all of them.”

_Or at least I hope so_, he added in a small voice.

They had left the street with food stalls and were now reminiscing at a fountain in a park.

“You can see the castle from here. I remember making sketches of it under the supervision of our teacher.”  

“Right… yours always were the best.”  

“Heh-heh, thank you for saying that.”

While it wasn’t as magnificent as a certain fountain in the country of the holy tree[1](https://re-library.com/translations/levelmaker/volume-19/side-story-21-seinforces-date-3-orgo-pov/#easy-footnote-bottom-1-118575), it was quite impressive in its own right. It was said that a past ruler had built it.

“Was this where you wanted to take me?”  

“Exactly, I remembered there should be several potential date spots around here.”  

“I see.”

Orgo turned around.

“Anyway, one of them should be over there. Let’s go.”  

“Alright.”

Where he was walking, there were many stores selling fashionable clothes and hats. The couple fit well into this place’s atmosphere.

“They seem to be selling many foreign looking[2](https://re-library.com/translations/levelmaker/volume-19/side-story-21-seinforces-date-3-orgo-pov/#easy-footnote-bottom-2-118575) clothes!”  

“Th-They do.”

The words “should we buy something?” were on the tip of his tongue, but sudden insecurity made him hesitate.

“There are many stores that let you try on clothes, are there not?”  

“F-For now, how about we look at them?”  

“And try it on if we see something we like?”  

“Of course.”

Myuri walked with a light gait. Orgo followed her as she took the lead, unaware of how rare that was for her.

“Look at this hat! What do you think?”  

“Right, I think it suits you.”

She was trying on a white hat with red feathers and a black ribbon attached to it. It meshed well with her blue hair.

“Oh, this one also looks nice!”  

“Right, it also suits you.”

This time, she tried on a modest necklace. It was made of something like animal fangs and looked somewhat flamboyant on her light skin.

“Hm~… Oh, look at this!”  

“Hm?”

Myuri picked a spiked, forbidding bracelet from a wagon and quickly put it onto Orgo’s arm.

“It suits you…”  

“Y-You think so?”  

“I do! But it does look a bit scary, so we should find something else.”  

“T-True.”

After that, they kept checking the stores. They looked at the clothes, tried some on, and then gave their impressions (though Orgo mostly kept to normative “it suits you”s).

Time passed as they did that. Finally, it was noon.

“Oh… These ones are nice! Wow…!”  

“Hm, what is it?”

She was looking at a pair of gloves. They were white with some light blue mixed in, as if specifically made for her.

“I wonder, should I buy them?”  

“Hrm… I-In that case…”  

“Huh?”  

“I-I’ll buy them.”

She gave him a blank look.

“You want to wear them…? I do not think they would suit you that much…”  

“N-No, you misunderstood! They’re for you… uhm… as a present.”  

“A present…?” She looked at the gloves and then back at him. “…You are aware that my birthday is not today, are you?”  

“I-I can give you a present, even if it isn’t your birthday, can’t I?”  

“Hm? But today is no anniversary of ours, either…”  

“That doesn’t matter!” Orgo replied impatiently to her understandable confusion.

He was afraid of losing this chance, after managing to say something that had been written in those books.

“…Are you sure?”  

“I-I guess. They’re not that expensive… and we’re on a date! I read that’s something people in a relationship do. Especially the men!”  

“I see! I-In that case, I shall take you up on your offer.”

Orgo, inwardly relieved, took the gloves hanging from the rack and brought them to the checkout.

“Could I get these?”  

“Of course… Are they a present for your girlfriend?” the employee asked with a smile.  

“Th-They are!”

The words sent a jolt[3](https://re-library.com/translations/levelmaker/volume-19/side-story-21-seinforces-date-3-orgo-pov/#easy-footnote-bottom-3-118575) through him, reminding him that they were on a date. He quickly paid for the gloves.

“Thank you for your patronage.”

The employee wrapped the gloves into pretty paper out of concern for the couple. Orgo gave his thanks and returned to Myuri.

“H-Here you go.”  

“Wow…! Thank you ever so much! I shall treasure them for the rest of my life!”  

“W-Well, unless you ask Alim for help, they won’t keep that long, right…? S-Still, I’m glad you like them.”  

“Eh-heh-heh.”

Appearing profoundly happy, she rubbed the wrapped-up gloves against her cheeks. He gazed at the scene.

“…Come to think of it, it’s noon already.”  

“It is true! Should we find a place to eat? This time, I will pay for it!”  

“Haven’t you heard? It’s usually the man who pays for the food when on a date. If everyone does that, I want to do it, too.”  

“…Does that not mean that dates are quite expensive for boys? It makes me feel bad.”  

“F-For me… uhm… it’s most important to make you happy, Myuri! Money doesn’t matter.”  

“…Eh-heh-heh.” Her cheeks flushed.

#### Footnotes:

1. Most likely the one from chapter 262.[](https://re-library.com/translations/levelmaker/volume-19/side-story-21-seinforces-date-3-orgo-pov/#easy-footnote-1-118575)

2. The original is 洋服 (“western-style clothes”) which doesn’t make much sense for natives to use, since for them “western style” might mean something else completely. I think they are the ones Alim popularized, so I guess it’s not impossible they’re using that word to describe specifically those kinds of clothes.[](https://re-library.com/translations/levelmaker/volume-19/side-story-21-seinforces-date-3-orgo-pov/#easy-footnote-2-118575)

3. The original is 地震 (“Earthquake”). This seems a bit weird and may be meant to be the homophone 自身 (“oneself”).[](https://re-library.com/translations/levelmaker/volume-19/side-story-21-seinforces-date-3-orgo-pov/#easy-footnote-3-118575)

+++

# Side Story 22 – Seinforce’s Date – 3 (Ruin PoV)

“Now that I look at it, are there more exhibitions here than there used to?” Lilo wondered.

The two of them had left the area of the park decorated with statues of past rulers, and were now in a section where several artworks were displayed.

“Hm, I can’t say for sure. You need permission from the country to display works of art here, so we might ask at the bureau later.”  

“Right.”

Ruin and Lilo walked around, looking at the artworks and appraising them, making use of their sensibilities as nobles and royalty.

“This Myrmecoleon statue is well-made.”  

“But it’s crude in some places… Alim could’ve done a lot better…”  

“Well, that’s because she’s Alim.”

They looked at another artwork.

“I wonder what this is supposed to express.”  

“…Hm~, happiness… maybe?”  

“Alim could’ve done a lot better…”  

“Well, that’s because she’s Alim.”

They kept looking at works of art, but their impressions repeatedly boiled down to “Alim could’ve done better.” They inadvertently broke into laughter.

“We’ve been influenced too much by her, haven’t we?” Lilo mused.  

“Ha-ha, we have. It probably can’t be helped…” Ruin agreed. “After all, we met her before she got this ridiculously strong.”  

“Such a precious memory…”

They both thought back to that day.

“…If she hadn’t been there back then… no, if she didn’t exist at all, what would have happened to us?” Lilo wondered.  

“No clue. All we can do is be grateful.”  

“You’re right.”

He looked at her face. She looked back at him. They each smiled.

“Want me to guess what you just thought, Ruin?”  

“Heh-heh, I’m sure you know me well enough.”  

“You were thinking, _at some point, they’ll erect a bronze statue of Alim in this park_… did I get it right?”  

“Full marks.”

If fact, this had been under discussion for quite some time at this point, but the two of them didn’t know that. After chuckling for a while, they decided to move to another spot.

“…That sounds interesting.”  

“I wonder what’s going on.”  

“It might be a street performer making a living with music.”  

“Oh, that makes sense.”

The two of them got closer to the supposed musician. It was quite the good performance and a crowd had formed. Only, the song ended right as they made it there.

“Thank you, thank you very much!”

“My, it’s already over,” Lilo commented in dejection.  

“Nothing we can do about that…”

When the people were about to leave, the musician spoke up once more.

“With everyone so excited, I shall play another song. This one will be a love song.”

Ruin, Lilo, and most of the other people who’d been about to leave stopped in their tracks and turned their attention back on the musician. The song that then played truly seemed a perfect match for the couple’s mental state and feelings.

“Woah… somehow, I can’t put it into words, but it’s wonderful…!”  

“Yes. I think it was a good call to go here for our date.”

Ruin unconsciously brought his hand close to Lilo’s again, which he had let go of earlier. She noticed and timidly took it. Then, the two of them temporarily got lost in their own world.

“-Thank you so much for listening.”

The musician bowed to the crowd.  

There was clapping. The loud sound brought the couple back to reality.

“What just happened…?”  

“…Is this what people mean by ‘getting lost in romantic feelings’?”  

“I-I’m not sure. For now, we should give a proper tip.”

Ruin put several silver coins he had on hand into the musician’s wooden box and then stepped back. The performer would later become famous, though at this point, no one could guess that.

“I’m sure there are other interesting things around here,” Ruin mused.  

“You’re right… Ah, it’s noon already, should we have lunch?”

A gaze at the clock showed that she was right. Ruin nodded.

“Let’s find a place… is there something you’d like to eat?”  

“No, I’m fine with anything.”  

“In that case… how about that one?”

Ruin was pointing at a chic café not far away, where you could see guests order sandwiches on the terrace.

“Sandwiches, huh…? Another of Alim’s boons.”  

“The only ones getting close to her cooking are master chefs. But it’s also nice to eat sandwiches in a normal place every now and then, right?”  

“Yeah.”

The two of them agreed on that, so they entered the restaurant and ordered plain sandwiches. Simple ones with just vegetables and ham.

“That reminds me, Ruin,” Lilo spoke up with slightly flushed cheeks while they were waiting for their order.  

“Hm? What is it?”  

“C-Can we go on another date in the future?”  

“Sure, if that’s what you want, Lilo… We can pick any day we’re not busy.”  

“I-In that case, how about I make lunch boxes the next time we go…? Though I never made those except for work.”  

“Really?”  

“Yes, I’m serious.”  

“I see… I’ll be looking forward to it.”

Shortly later, their sandwiches arrived. Lilo did her best to commit the taste to memory, as a benchmark for what she had to overcome with her cooking.

+++

# 590 – What To Do

“…So, that’s what happened, Your Majesty.”

I was telling King Mephilad what had occurred with King Rama the other day. I mean, I was a citizen of this country, so it was better to discuss it before getting more deeply involved with another nation.

“I see. To think he’d make such a request.”  

“Indeed. For that reason, I was thinking of crafting this scepter-like weapon the day after tomorrow, based on the drawing in the book King Rama showed me.”

Back then, I had also recreated the Hero’s Sword based on old literature. Though my Divine Sword was still stronger in any aspect. Well divine grade items were incomparable to anything below.

“I see. Although it is one of Anazumu’s three leading countries, they have been without their signature weapon[1](https://re-library.com/translations/levelmaker/volume-19/chapter-590-what-to-do/#easy-footnote-bottom-1-118579) for a long time, and they expressed that it harmed their country’s dignity.”

The king was unexpectedly nonchalant about it. Well, Mephilad was on friendly terms with Bufura, so he probably felt safe enough. If this was the country of the holy tree, his reaction likely would’ve been very different.

It was the same for me. I wasn’t willing to give that country even one iota of assistance, after their king treated Kanata and the others so poorly.

“Putting that aside, Alim, the part that caught my attention was how you restored those books.”  

“…Oh, I can guess where this is going.”  

“Exactly… could we ask you for that?”

The Mephilad Kingdom also had many books that were in a poor state. Back when I went through the libraries to copy all the information from the books into the Tozumaho, I excluded the places storing damaged literature… This might be a good opportunity to update the information on the device.

“Understood, I’ll take care of it.”  

“Please do… Since we gave you unrestricted access to all libraries in the past, I assume you know where they are?”  

“Yes, every last one!”

_I spent quite some time there, so I’m familiar enough with them to work there at this point. Only, while I gathered a veritable treasure trove of information, it’s such a pain to read through it all. Even so, there’s work to be done._

“Ah, before you leave, spend some time with Karua, will you?”  

“Eh-heh-heh, that was the plan, Your Majesty.”

Our first priority when coming to the castle was always to spend time with the princess.

“No need to rush crafting the weapon, you can do the book restoration whenever want. Just inform me before you get to work.”  

“Will do, Your Majesty!”

Thus, we moved to Karua’s room. The number of toys and games she had available had increased in recent times. The other day, we played Kendama, and before that, it was Karuta[2](https://re-library.com/translations/levelmaker/volume-19/chapter-590-what-to-do/#easy-footnote-bottom-2-118579).

In any case, she already knew that we were from another world, so I could bring her whatever I wanted. The ultimate goal was to introduce her to video games.

“With all that said, what should we play today, Karua?”  

“What about Shogi? I finally understand how the rooks and bishops are used!”  

“Oh… Shogi? That’s fine for me.”

This world had Chess, but not Shogi. The main difference between the two games was that in the latter, you would gain control of any enemy game-pieces you captured.

“Turning defeated soldiers into allies and fighting with them does sound like something from a story.”  

“But in exchange, your original allies may also betray you…”  

“Th-That is also true!”

In a resemblance of what I did often, Karua puffed out her cheeks. Almost by reflex, Mika smushed them with her hands. In reaction, the princess pinched my cheeks, likely since that chain of events had reminded her of how wonderful they felt.

“Recently, I never had any opportunity to touch your cheeks, Alim. They feel just as wonderful as they used to.”

At this point, I didn’t even try to resist.

“Now, let us play Shogi already!”

Thus, we got ready for our match. It apparently didn’t matter to Karua that games like Chess and Shogi didn’t depend on chance; she still enjoyed them. We had played the Game of Life several times, but Karua almost always ended up in first place thanks to her extreme luck.

“That reminds me, Alim, has your work situation calmed down?”  

“As a matter of fact, it has.”

The biggest advantage of this world lacking good means of transportation was probably that I wasn’t expected to travel to other cities or countries. If it had, I’d likely be jetting around the world right now.

_Thinking about it, isn’t King Rama the very first client asking me to come to another country[3](https://re-library.com/translations/levelmaker/volume-19/chapter-590-what-to-do/#easy-footnote-bottom-3-118579)?_

He was the most ardent fan among royals I’d met so far… This man, just how many of my firsts was he going to claim?

“Alim, let us start already!”  

“Ah, sorry.”

_I got lost in thought._

Karua would go first and I second. Mika just watched. The princess made the first move.

#### Footnotes:

1. The original is 「者」の武器 (“weapon of ‘person'”). I assume it’s meant in the meaning of “weapon the specific person (the guide) unique to the country is using”.[](https://re-library.com/translations/levelmaker/volume-19/chapter-590-what-to-do/#easy-footnote-1-118579)

2. [Kendama](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kendama) is the Japanese of version of the Cup-and-Ball game. [Karuta](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Karuta) are Japanese playing cards, originally based on Portuguese ones.[](https://re-library.com/translations/levelmaker/volume-19/chapter-590-what-to-do/#easy-footnote-2-118579)

3. No, that was King Mephilad asking him to go fight Surtr. Also, King Rama didn’t ask him to come to Bufura, he would’ve sent the book to Mephilad.[](https://re-library.com/translations/levelmaker/volume-19/chapter-590-what-to-do/#easy-footnote-3-118579)

+++

# 591 – Indra, Vajra of the Guide

“Anyway, today I’m going to craft this thing I was commissioned for!”

I had reached a good stopping point for this week’s work, so I’d quickly make it. Though thinking about it another way, recreating something based on ancient literature[1](https://re-library.com/translations/levelmaker/volume-19/chapter-591-indra-vajra-of-the-guide/#easy-footnote-bottom-1-118999) also qualified as important work.

“Do you know what it’s made of?” Mika asked.  

“Not everything, only that Phantom Ore and Orichalcum are some of the materials. It’s different from the Hero’s Sword where all I needed was a hilt and Orichalcum. That’s why I’ll start by recreating it with Dark Matter.”  

“I see… I hope it goes well!”  

“Thanks”

I retreated into the magic room that served as my smithy. The last time I was here was when I upgraded everyone’s weapons to divine grade.

I immediately created the Vajra with Dark Matter and then appraised it. It looked like the weapon was focused on lightning magic. But the only one specializing in that kind of magic I knew other than me was Shuu’s acquaintance, Thor.

_…Huh? Is this thing made for me…? I’m getting a bad feeling, but I’m sure it’s just coincidence. Exactly, that must be it._

Other than serving as a strong catalyst for lighting magic, the weapon didn’t seem different from Gungnir and the Hero’s Sword. Though it also said that its name was “Indra[2](https://re-library.com/translations/levelmaker/volume-19/chapter-591-indra-vajra-of-the-guide/#easy-footnote-bottom-2-118999)“.

While the Hero’s Sword was nameless, the Sage’s Spear, Gungnir, had a proper name for a legendary weapon. I got the feeling that “Indra” wasn’t a weapon name. Well, that was what it said, nothing to be done about it.

_I wondered about that before, but why is it so easy to recreate stuff like the Hero’s Sword with Dark Matter? Isn’t it weird that it’s so simple to create something on the upper end of legend grade? Well, worrying about that won’t do me any good. I was even able to create copies of a movie that hadn’t aired on Earth yet._

“Now…”

This was a request from the ruler of a country, so I couldn’t just let my skills do everything and call it a day. I had to craft it properly by hand[3](https://re-library.com/translations/levelmaker/volume-19/chapter-591-indra-vajra-of-the-guide/#easy-footnote-bottom-3-118999). I took out the required materials from the pouch I used for storage. Then, I made it from scratch.

_That reminds me, I never put some kind of brand on the weapons I made._

Up to this point, I only made legend grade weapons for Gilmars, Parasuna, and the S- and SS-Rank adventurers the former introduced to me.

_Should I have used some kind of brand when I did that? At this point, it’s probably too late. In that case, I’ll continue without one._

_____  

___  

_

_Phew, I’m done._

It turned out exactly the same as the prototype made with Dark Matter.  

_Tee-hee…! Only thing left is to deliver it._

“Mika~, I’ll be going out for a bit.”  

“Huh? You’re going by yourself this time?”  

“You can tag along if you want, but I wasn’t planning to stay there for long.”  

“That’s fine! I’ll join you in case something happens!”  

“Alright.”

Thus, Mika and I went to Kanata and asked him to send us to the Bufura Kingdom again.

Incidentally, it looked like he was currently studying medical sciences. Before that, it had been finances and law. He was probably also planning to go over statecraft and psychology.  

_Just what is he going to become in the future?_

It also affected Sakura, who was tagging along with him, in a bad way. When she muttered “Kanata keeps looking at pictures of naked girls that aren’t me. Though I understand he has to, since it’s to study medicine,” in complaint, Mika shot back an “In that case, you’ll have to go further with him, Sakura,” which the younger sister rejected with teary eyes and a bright red face. It was rather funny to watch.

“Alright, we’re back!”  

“He sent us to another backstreet alley. Let’s get out of here quickly.”

We didn’t want to get accosted by thugs like last time, so Mika and I quickly left the alley and made our way to the castle. At the gates, we showed our adventurer cards. The guards let us in happily once they learned who we were.

“Oh, Alim! It is good to see you,” King Rama exclaimed. “Does that mean you finished the Vajra?”  

“It does, Your Majesty! Here it is.”

I handed the weapon, which was wrapped in a piece of cloth, to the king.

“So, this is it… Our country’s…”

Given his personality, I expected him to show a grin when my hand touched his in the process, but that never happened. Was he too focused on the weapon itself?

“Wonderful. Thank you so much, Alim… We can see that it is as well-crafted as one would expect from you, but just to make sure, We shall have it appraised.”

After saying that, the king called Hanuman and carefully handed the weapon to him. The guard took it, gave a bow, and then left the room.

“Anyway, thanks to your earlier assistance, Alim, the investigation has progressed quite a bit in those few days.”  

“That’s good to hear!”  

“Indeed, we now know who Our great-grandfather gave the privilege of being the Guide. Are you interested?”

I had assisted them up to this point, so I couldn’t deny being somewhat curious.

“Could you tell us about it, Your Majesty?”  

“Of course, We shall do so… Follow Us.”

#### Footnotes:

1. The original is 過去の分権 (“ancient decentralization of authority”). Since 分権 is a homophone of 文献 (“literature”), I assume that’s an error.[](https://re-library.com/translations/levelmaker/volume-19/chapter-591-indra-vajra-of-the-guide/#easy-footnote-1-118999)

2. The original is インドラ (indora). [Indra](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Indra) is a deity from Hinduism.[](https://re-library.com/translations/levelmaker/volume-19/chapter-591-indra-vajra-of-the-guide/#easy-footnote-2-118999)

3. If the result is 100% the same, I don’t really see the meaning. I guess it’s similar to natural and artificial vanilla, where both are identical, but people still want the natural.

+++

# 592 – The Guide of the Past

“Normally, no one except for chief vassals are allowed to enter this place. Well, you and Mika, are an exception.”

We were in King Rama’s study. Different from the small library we’d visited the other day, this was clearly the king’s private space. For some reason, visiting an older man’s quarters made me nervous.

I checked out the bookshelves after entering the study:  

_…Alim Nariwei in a miniskirt._  

_…Special Edition: The angels of the party ‘The Earth’._  

_…Limited Edition: Alim Nariwei in an apron._

It was a collection of photos from Mika and me. I only took a short glance, but there were many more other than those just mentioned. Moreover, many of them were awfully rare.

During the photoshoot for the “Limited Edition: Alim Nariwei in an apron”, there had been an idiot among the staffers, suggesting I do the “naked apron”. I obviously declined. If I remembered correctly, the miniskirt one was drawn in a way that extremely emphasized my tights. Thinking back on it, they were also very focused on my socks. My legs weren’t even that plump to begin with.

_I just don’t get how men think._

I preferred the easy-to-understand ones like Shuu. Still, when I turned back into a man, I definitely had such idiosyncrasies, too. It was complicated.

“Oh, you found Our photo collection of you and Mika, Alim… We use this room to store almost everything that has been published about you up to this point. This includes specials and limited editions.”

_Hah, so he’s got practically everything._  

It was hard to tell what a rich person obsessed with idols would do. If only they would stop at collecting photos.

“Unfortunately, We never managed to get Our hands on the limited edition ‘War Alim’. That one was sold for such a short time, and the demand was too high.”

The king seemed rather dejected when he said that. I usually kept everything in my pouch, in case something like this happened.

“Let me check… I have that one with me currently, do you want it?”  

“What!? I-If possible, could you sell it to Us after signing it? We shall pay you 100’000 bells for it!”  

“N-No need to go that far. Just pay me the normal price it was going for…”

While we were in the middle of something important, he seemed happy about it, so it wasn’t a bad thing. It would probably make dealing with him in the future easier. I signed the “Limited Edition: War Alim” on the cover where the king indicated and then gave it to him.

“We shall keep this as an heirloom!”  

“If you’re going to make something an heirloom, it should be the Vajra.”  

“…That one is a national treasure, not a personal heirloom.”

King Rama seemed both happy and solemn as he put the magazine onto the bookshelf. Then, his expression immediately turned serious, and he continued speaking.

“…So, as for the diary’s contents.”  

“What did it say?”  

“The one being named the Guide apparently wasn’t born in this country.”  

“I-I see.”

Just like wolfkin could only give away one Pledge of Loyalty in their lives, the members of King Rama’s lineage could only designate one Guide. And while common belief had been that no past king in several hundred years had designated a Guide, the current king’s great-grandfather had done so… at least according to the diary. Exactly since the crucial information about said Guide was missing, I had been tasked with restoring the diary. Which led us to the present. And now King Rama told us that a foreigner had been made the Guide.

“What kind of person were they?”  

“From what is written… it was a man capable of strange feats without using special items or skills. Feeling inner strength from him, Our great grandfather decided to make him the Guide, something he could do only once in his life…” King Rama frowned before continuing. “Our grandfather often told us that his father could be an irresponsible man, but to think he went this far.”  

“Ah-ha-ha-ha.”  

“If it was Us, We would surely name you the Guide, Alim.”

After reading this diary, he might just decide to go and make me the guide. I should change the subject.

“Do you know anything more about this man?”  

“He apparently worked at the side of Our great grandfather for some time before suddenly leaving for the Mephilad Kingdom… He kept muttering things like ‘I want to return to my homeland’. He was quite talented at making people laugh, which Our great grandfather seemed to like about him, but at the times when he muttered this wish, his expression was said to be awfully lonesome.”

_Huh… his home country?_

While Anazumu was quite a bit smaller than Earth, distances still could be substantial, so it was likely quite hard for him to find his way home. Maybe there was a means of returning home for him in the Mephilad Kingdom[1](https://re-library.com/translations/levelmaker/volume-19/chapter-592-the-guide-of-the-past/#easy-footnote-bottom-1-119002).

“We’d like to make you the Guide after all, Alim.”  

“You can’t. I am already the Hero!”  

“True, hah.”

King Rama dropped his shoulders in dejection.  

_If this topic drags on, he’ll never stop. I better change the subject again._

“Do you know anything else at this point?”  

“No, that was all We learned.”

_It doesn’t sound like they’ve gotten very far. Well, it’s only been three days since I fixed the book, so that’s to be expected._

#### Footnotes:

1. Another case of a surprise being spoiled by an earlier chapter, since chapter 565 already told us who the guide is. Also, Anazumu is apparently smaller than Earth. I wonder if it’s still a globe or works on different prinziples

+++

# 593 – Books

A day had passed since I managed to deliver the Vajra to King Rama without incident. They were apparently still in the middle of their investigation but had learned quite a few things already.

So, today I’d fix the old books King Mephilad asked me to. Thinking that this, once again, might give various new insights made me somewhat happy.  

_Maybe I should take this opportunity to study up on Anazumu’s history for real… Nah, that’d be too much work._

If I were to study, it would be better to pick something that was useful on Earth, like what Kanata did. For now, I would work hard so I could copy those books into the Tozumaho.

For the first time in ages, I went to the library on my own. It was a large building close to the castle, which consequently also meant that it was close to my mansion. Despite gaining the right to freely access everything there, I had only gone to the place a single time[1](https://re-library.com/translations/levelmaker/volume-19/chapter-593-books/#easy-footnote-bottom-1-119004). With my abilities, I was probably the person who could stay in the same place without leaving for the longest time. The goal back then had been to stuff all the information into the Tozumaho.

Still, there were tons of people in the library. The building was one of the few recreational facilities in the city, so that was to be expected. I made my way to the deepest depths of the building, where several important archives were located.

This was the only part I hadn’t gone to during my prior visit. It housed tomes that were tattered and abnormally old, but still important. This was now my destination. They probably put a lot of trust in me for letting me enter without supervision.

To begin, I prepared multiple sprayers filled with the restoration fluid I’d used the other day and then created dozens of robots. I attached a sprayer to each of those and activated them. As for me, I was holding something like a shower head. Even if the restoration fluid were to soak the pages, it would merely restore them, not make them wet. Thus, hosing them down with a shower head was quite efficient. The robots were there to take care of the books I missed.

I immediately turned on the flow. Every single book that was hit became pristine.  

_But even using that method, it still takes forever. Oh well, better keep it up._

While I was at it, I also cleaned the room and the bookshelves themselves. Or rather, some of the robots did, using cleaning fluid. Well, it was part of the service I offered. Anyway, while it did take time, I went at it at hyper-speed, so by normal standards I was done quickly.

_Now what, should I just copy them into the Tozumaho? No one is here and I’m not under surveillance, so I could do it right now if I wanted. Hm~… I feel bad about this[2](https://re-library.com/translations/levelmaker/volume-19/chapter-593-books/#easy-footnote-bottom-2-119004)…_

_I guess I’ll hold off for another time. I can just ask the king when I actually need the information in the Tozumaho._

Thus, I stored away the robots and left the library to inform the king.

_____  

___  

_

“You worked as fast as expected.”  

“Thank you for saying that, Your Majesty.”  

“I’ll pay you at a later time… Are you truly fine with that compensation?”

He knew that I wasn’t hurting for money, so he likely brought it up deliberately.  

_Well, if he wants me to be frank…_

“How about we say that you owe me a favor instead?”  

“I feel like it wouldn’t be the first, but that should work.”  

“In that case, let’s settle it this way.”

Though I didn’t expect to actually cash in said favor.

“Still, thanks to you, Alim, we’ll be able to learn a lot about the past. You restored the ancient historical records, and for the events spanning the last 300 years[3](https://re-library.com/translations/levelmaker/volume-19/chapter-593-books/#easy-footnote-bottom-3-119004) or so, we can consult with Princess Elle and the Hero Herrell. This will advance our historical research.”

_Research, huh…? In that case, I should probably also give the king the same offer I made the other day._

“Would you like to borrow these, then?”

I brought out glasses of the same kind I had shown King Rama and repeated my explanation.

“…Convenient. I’d like to borrow three pairs.”  

“Of course, here you go.” I handed him the glasses.

_Maybe it is time to make those more widely available? I could probably talk to the people from the Medial Merchant Association about mass producing them. Hang on, they’re legend grade. I’m the only one who can make them._

“Alright! I’ll be going home for the day, then.”  

“Hrm, you’re not going to spend time with Karua?”  

“No, I feel somewhat tired today.”  

“Of course, I forgot. You must be, after restoring countless books. Go home and rest for the day.”  

“I will. Till another time, Your Majesty.”

Thus, while feeling sorry for not dropping in on the princess, I went home. There, Mika greeted me.

“Welcome back! Would you like dinner? Or a bath? Or maybe… me?”  

“I’m tired today, so I’ll go to bed after eating and taking a bath.”  

“A-Alright… Hmph!” she replied grumpily.

It looked adorable, so I gave her a hug.

#### Footnotes:

1. It’s “several times” in the original. I’m pretty sure he went there exactly once to copy everything.[](https://re-library.com/translations/levelmaker/volume-19/chapter-593-books/#easy-footnote-1-119004)

2. Why stop at this point? It’s clear they trust him with this information, or they wouldn’t send him to fix those books without supervision.[](https://re-library.com/translations/levelmaker/volume-19/chapter-593-books/#easy-footnote-2-119004)

3. It’s 100 years in the original. I’m pretty sure the events of the prior emergence of the demon god happened 300 years before the story.

# 594 – Everyday

The two weeks mostly spent on restoring books and getting a deeper understanding of history had ended, and we were back on Earth. Mika and I didn’t have anything planned so far for this week.

The intra scholastic tournament was next week, so Shuu had ramped up his training, and Kanata and Sakura would apparently go on a date at the Zoo next Sunday. Anyway, we didn’t have anything planned and no good ideas had come to me, so that was what was on my mind right now.

Still, it was hard to come up with something. I was at the end of my rope concerning how to spend time with Mika. Moreover, a little over four months from now, the second year of high school would end. I had to find ways to have fun and make out with Mika during that time. Once the third year of high school started, we’d be busy studying for entrance exams[1](https://re-library.com/translations/levelmaker/volume-19/chapter-594-everyday/#easy-footnote-bottom-1-119027).

And while our school was combined with a grade- and middle school, with even a university technically being connected to it, which should make it easy to get in one of the better universities after finishing high school, we couldn’t get negligent. On that note, said grade-, middle-, and high schools plus the connected university were said to be among the most demanding in the country.

Come to think of it, it had only been around two and a half months since we came home from Anazumu. If you summed up the combined time on Earth and in Anazumu, almost a year had passed for me since I first arrived in the other world. Thinking about it, so many things happened… way too many. Surely, I would never experience another such eventful year.

_Not good. Right now, I shouldn’t think back on the past, I need to come up with a way to spend time with Mika this week. Most important among that our next date on Sunday._

_…We got those tickets that let us enter for free, so maybe we should go to the circus again, just as the two of us? From what I heard, it would stay here until mid-December. But on second thought, we just went there last week on this side, so that won’t work. What to do, what to do…_

“Ayumu, is something wrong?” Mika was peering at my face.

Right now, we were on our way to school. She likely asked me since I seemed as if my mind was far away. She looked adorable. It made me want to ravish her right here.

“Ah, no, I was just thinking. About what we could do this week.”  

“It’s fall, so let’s go gather mushrooms!”  

“Mushrooms… hm~. It might be dangerous if we pick any poisonous ones. How about we gather grapes instead?”  

“Let’s do that!”

After quickly dismissing the idea of gathering mushrooms, we settled on grapes instead. In the end, if we talked it out together, we usually came up with decent plans.  

_Gathering grapes is a nice idea. Though it was mine to begin with._

On third thought, we hadn’t spent any time looking at the leaves changing color this year. Maybe we could do this on that outing, too.

“If we had more time, we could go to a hot spring inn and enjoy the scenery of fall, just as the two of us,” Mika mused.  

“But we don’t… Grr.”  

“Exactly. Staying in a place with a mixed open-air bath and then taking baths as the two of us… Eh-heh.”

And then crawling under the covers next to each other, while not wearing anything, and get intimate.

Time certainly was an issue, but we didn’t have that much money saved up either. Staying at a hot spring inn would be a hard ask.

“Well, gathering grapes will be enough for this week!”  

“Yeah!”

The most important part was to have fun. We could feed each other the grapes.

“With that settled, we’ll have to work hard this week, right?”  

“Right!”

We walked to our school with linked hands, as always. Likely since everyone was used to it at this point, there were no snide comments. After boarding the train while staying vigilant, we started talking again.

“Oh, Ayumu, you got these tickets, right? Couldn’t we go to the circus again?”

It looked like Mika had the same idea.

“I was also thinking of doing that.”  

“Makes sense. Not using them would be such a waste.”

Circuses didn’t stay in the same place for long. We had to use the tickets while we still had the chance. Looking at it another way, they hardly made up for all the trouble the man had caused us… Well, it was the thought the counted.

“What wrong, Ayumu? You’re looking so grave. Wanna touch my chest?”  

“If I fondle your chest while we’re on the train, people will think I’m a groper. Let’s do that when we’re back home.”  

“…Eh-heh-heh, that’s fine.”

_Me looking grave? That’s not good._

In any case, I didn’t expect to talk about making out on the train today. It took me so much by surprise, I ended up being unable to resist and actually touching her chest. Even Mika, who had been the one to tell me to do it, was blinking in surprise.

“Ah, we’ve arrived.”

Afterwards, we simply continued walking to school while holding hands.

_Walking to school together, deciding on what to do on dates and talking about pervy things… spending our everyday peacefully like this is nice, too._  

_Well, what counts as “everyday” is different for everyone. Other people seeing us probably think we’re way too lovey-dovey. Tee-hee._

---

**Author’s note:**  

Turns out the intra scholastic Judo tournament is usually around August. I wrote this without doing much research. Incidentally, the current events are in the middle of November, and Shuu’s tournament will be at the end of it.

Let this be a lesson for the future.

# 595 – Towards the Tournament – 1 (Shuu)

“Phew… hah… phew…”

Even I ended up getting somewhat winded on the final stretch. The intra scholastic tournament would already be next week, so I obviously started training daily for it. I mean, normally you’d start training three weeks… no, even a month before, but I got complacent because of my abilities.

Strictly speaking, there was also the time in Anazumu, so the training I put in was probably several times more than what the other team members did, but from an outside perspective it undoubtedly looked as if I was slacking off.

Over there, Ayumu prepared a magic room wherein time was sped up and robots who’d serve as training partners for me (not sure how he did it, but he even included the data of an Olympic athlete who got gold). This obviously made a world of difference.

Thanks to that, I probably got a lot stronger. At the end, I managed to score at least one point on every robot. I was grateful to my friend, just as I was grateful to Rir for helping me and testing my skills.

I probably wouldn’t have any skill or experience issues. My abilities were what got me this far.

Incidentally, my Martial Arts skills were currently inactive. When we came back to Earth, my fighting skills started to activate on their own and (according to Kanata) there was currently no way other than deactivating them completely[1](https://re-library.com/translations/levelmaker/volume-19/chapter-595-towards-the-tournament-1-shuu/#easy-footnote-bottom-1-119029)… but even without them, I could feel how much stronger I had gotten.

That said, I didn’t get why Ayumu suddenly came and asked “How about we include other fighting styles? It might help!” before installing all kinds of combat data on the robots and making me fight them. In the end, I learned a ton of new things.

“Man… I can’t believe you’re messing around with your girlfriend right before the tournament. Just what is this?” Gouda, the vice club head complained. “You’ve clearly gotten stronger than you were last week. I couldn’t even see your moves.”

_He couldn’t see my moves…? Huh, guess it’s gotten that far._

“What did you do?” he asked.  

“Eh… I mean, just trainin’ in private with her…”  

“Oh, so you’re training by the two of you without coming to the club room… Techniques to pin someone down, for example…”  

“I know what you’re thinkin’, but you’re way off.”

_Not good. For a moment, I thought he found out what we do on the other side, even though that shouldn’t be impossible. This ain’t good at all._

On the surface, I was your standard high schooler, which meant they could never find out that I had already crossed that line[2](https://re-library.com/translations/levelmaker/volume-19/chapter-595-towards-the-tournament-1-shuu/#easy-footnote-bottom-2-119029).

“I was wondering about that before, but how far have you and Fún gone?” Gouda asked.  

“Oh, I’m curious about that, too!” another team member joined in.  

“Same here!”  

“Wha-!?”

_Why are these guys so interested in that? No choice. Guess I’ll play it down somewhat._

“…We went on a date in the amusement park, and we kissed. Happy now?”  

“Whoa!”

_Damn you, Gouda. I’ll throw you later._

“It’s not my place to speak about someone’s girlfriend,” a younger team member commented, “but Fún is just so sexy.”  

“True, she is. I keep looking where I shouldn’t…”

Whether these guys were looking at her chest or legs, their gazes were weird.

“Why you…” I growled.  

“Eek… the club head who never loses his temper looks like he’s about to blow his top…”  

“I’m more exasperated than angry.”  

“Well, I get it. I apologize, so please forgive me.”

Rir was popular among the boys, and they couldn’t help themselves, so I decided to overlook it. On the contrary, it made me feel somewhat proud of my girlfriend.

“I’ll say… hah, you’re strong, Fún.”  

“You think so? Thank you, Instructor!”

On the other hand, there was Gorilla Sensei who made this comment as he seemed to watch over Rir. She was training with me, so it was only natural for her to grow stronger.

“Gouda, come here for a moment.”  

“What is it?”

When he was called, Gouda put down his sports drink and went to our instructor.

“Go one round against Fún.”  

“Against her?”  

“Yes.”

Gouda shot me a glance.  

_Gorilla Sensei asked him to, so it can’t be helped… Guess I’ll signal him with my eyes that he’s in for it if he tries anythin’ weird._

Likely picking up on my thoughts, Gouda’s face twitched slightly as he nodded.

“If you would, Gouda!” Rir told him.  

“R-Right,” he replied sheepishly.

The two of them got ready in the spot designated by Gorilla Sensei and then started the match. By common sense, Rir was at an overwhelming disadvantage. There was the height and weight difference, and, more fundamentally, the difference in gender. And there was also a difference in experience.

However…

“As I thought.”  

“…What?”

She had thrown Gouda.

“S-She got him!?”  

“No way!?”

Gorilla Sensei didn’t seem surprised. He must’ve already noticed it. While she was a beginner at Judo, she trained with me, her existing affinity for martial arts and fighting skills helped perfect her abilities, and being from a warrior race, she could exhibit high physical abilities… Even I didn’t think I could perceive all her movements.

“…Gouda is by no means a weak fighter. On the contrary, he has the abilities to be entrusted the role of vice-captain, even if we were to make it to the countrywide tournament. That’s the reason he’s the vice club head… This is Fún’s affinity for physical activities[3](https://re-library.com/translations/levelmaker/volume-19/chapter-595-towards-the-tournament-1-shuu/#easy-footnote-bottom-3-119029). If you ask me, it isn’t just Judo but all kinds of sports. If she had come to this school earlier, she’d surely already be registered as an athlete.”

Gouda looked at Rir and me, still dumbfounded.

Maybe that was what Gorilla Sensei had been aiming for…

“Also, I assume that she really did train with Hino[4](https://re-library.com/translations/levelmaker/volume-19/chapter-595-towards-the-tournament-1-shuu/#easy-footnote-bottom-4-119029) daily. I think that was what caused her talent in Judo to bloom.”  

“I see… I did hear several times that she beat a girl from the track and field club by a wide margin.”

Gouda stood up with a remorseful look. Then, he stared at me.

“You’ll help us, right, Club Head?”  

“Obviously.”

Gorilla Sensei had managed to stir up the crowd and lift morale.

# 596 – Towards the Competition – 2 (Shuu)

“Anyway, thanks for your hard work.”  

“Likewise… thanks for going along.”  

“No worries. We fight as a team, so ain’t that only natural?”  

“You might be right there.”

Rir and I left the club room. Well, we’d probably come back here tomorrow anyway. As usual, she refrained from giving me a hug after club activities.

“I can’t believe it… I thought I’d never be able to keep up with you, Shuu, and now I surpassed everyone else…”  

“Well, you got impressive reflexes, and I also gave you one-on-one trainin’ in Anazumu. Would be more surprisin’ if you didn’t get better.”  

“Woof, that’s true!”

That said, I’d been the one most surprised. Maybe smart people did learn all kinds of things at a faster pace than normal folk, after all. Come to think of it, Rir managed to outperform club members in all sports.

“Hey, Rir. Is it true that you beat a girl from the track and field club on the 100-meter dash?”  

“It is! I mean, everyone keeps saying that I’m the most amazing at PE. Regardless of the curricle.”  

“I think you mean curriculum, not curricle[1](https://re-library.com/translations/levelmaker/volume-19/chapter-596-towards-the-competition-2-shuu/#easy-footnote-bottom-1-119031). Ain’t that a good thing?”  

“…But surpassing people who work so hard at clubs as if it was nothing… uhm, it feels bad…”

_Huh, so did she feel like that today, too?_

Bringing down a judo practitioner with that much of a weight advantage was impressive. It was something she should brag about.

“You gotta be prouder of yourself. You’re genuinely amazin’.”  

“Y-You think so?”  

“You’re good at both studyin’ and exercisin’; pretty much a model student… Sooner or later, someone’s gonna show up, thinkin’ I’m a poor match for you as your boyfriend.”  

“Huh… It’s more that I drag you down…”  

“That ain’t it.”  

“Woof?”

She inclined her head in confusion. Although we didn’t hug, that didn’t stop us from walking so close together, we were almost touching, which caused her head to slightly rest on my shoulder.  

_Gah, she’s so damn cute._

“Will you be going to bed right after taking a bath and eating dinner today?”  

“That was the plan. Somethin’ you wanna do?”  

“Something I’d like to do? Well… uhm… I’d like to talk and spend some more time with you, but…”

I also felt like something was missing currently. The only times we got to hug was in the morning and when we went to school. I got hooked on how nice it felt and now I somehow couldn’t calm down. At this point, she had completely stolen my heart.

“In that case, come to my room later. We can spend time together as long as we keep it under an hour.”  

“Awoo! I’m so happy! Shuu, uhm… ever since we did it on this side, you were the one to initiate several times, right?”  

“Guess so?”

From my perspective, it was more like the things holding me back had disappeared. Emotionally, it had become much easier to bring it up with her. It was like I no longer had to restrain myself… As an experiment, I suggested having sex twice in Anazumu, and she accepted both times happily with her tail wagging. Was that what it meant to sink into carnal desires?

Like Ayumu and Mika? Not exactly, but I definitely started thinking that loving each other might be all we needed, which seemed unlike me. Or maybe it meant that I finally gained a profound understanding of how important she was to me? Well, it didn’t matter in the end. The simple truth was that I loved her. That was all.

And it was probably all thanks to my best friend.

“In that case, you can touch me as much as you want today… We might also do it during that hour…”  

“A-Ah… nah, that’d probably tire us out too much.”

Maybe due to the sweat, she looked strangely alluring, almost causing me to give in to my base desires. Not good.

“In that case, I’ll touch the parts I like most about you, Shuu[2](https://re-library.com/translations/levelmaker/volume-19/chapter-596-towards-the-competition-2-shuu/#easy-footnote-bottom-2-119031)…”  

“About that… well, be my guest.”

_What am I sayin’? Guess I let go of most my self-restraint, after all… I might be turnin’ into a huge pervert. Question is, am I growin’ up or regressin’? Wasn’t I worried ’bout not bein’ able to do it before? This is hard._

“What will we do once the intra scholastic tournament is over?”  

“That’ll probably be around Christmas… We could go on a date somewhere.”  

“I was hoping for you to say that! Eh-heh-heh.”

_Dang… too cute…_

_With how things are goin’, might as well win the countrywide competition and then go on the date in high spirits. It should be possible! It might sound like wishful thinkin’, but with my current skills, I can do it!_

_Hang on… what ’bout money? Let’s see… do I have enough for Christmas, gifts and everythin’? I do have some leeway, but at this rate, what I saved up from part-time jobs won’t be enough. I also gotta think ’bout the other side._

“Awoo, I can’t wait~… huh!?”

She suddenly turned to look behind us. She kept staring there.

“Rir, is somethin’ wrong?”  

“Well… I felt like I heard the sound of suspicious footsteps.”  

“Suspicious footsteps…?”  

“Yeah… But there’s no one there, so I guess I must’ve misheard.”

She turned to me while still glaring in the same direction.

_I see, she thought there was some suspicious guy who might be dangerous._

We kept looking around on high alert, as we boarded the train on the station and made our way home. My old man was there, so it was the safest place possible.

#### Footnotes:

1. In the original, she mixes up 樹木 (“trees and shrubs”) and 種目 (“item”, “event”), which are almost homophones, with just one syllable slightly different.[](https://re-library.com/translations/levelmaker/volume-19/chapter-596-towards-the-competition-2-shuu/#easy-footnote-1-119031)

2. I don’t think it sounded that suggestive in the original. Also, I’m pretty sure she’s talking about his muscles.[](https://re-library.com/translations/levelmaker/volume-19/chapter-596-towards-the-competition-2-shuu/#easy-footnote-2-119031)

# Side Story 23 – Seinforce’s Date – 4 (Orgo PoV)

“That was delicious!”  

“Happy to hear that.”

Orgo had paid for both of them in the restaurant. Just as the date-manual had said.

“Going on a date is so much fun! Like when we played just by the two of us.”  

“You got a point there… well, going on a date still is different in some ways, isn’t it?”  

“You think so?”

They were talking as they walked through the streets again. Killing time while frequently looking at shops and stalls. Myuri was still half a step behind Orgo.

“Which shop should we look at next? How about the one over there?”  

“That one?”

Where Myuri was pointing stood a pet shop. Orgo considered it a good idea and decided to go there with her.

“So cute. Would you look at that Ododo chick? It is adorable!”  

“What was I supposed to say again in such a situation again? Y-You’re much more adorable-”  

“Oh, rabbits!”

He sighed in relief when he saw her enjoy herself, likely having accustomed to the thought of being on a date. It helped him calm down. The couple left the pet shop and started walking again.

“It might be nice to have a pet.”  

“But there’s already lots of horses at the castle.”  

“That might be true… I am hardly a specialist on horses, but would they be able to get along[1](https://re-library.com/translations/levelmaker/volume-19/side-story-23-seinforces-date-4-orgo-pov/#easy-footnote-bottom-1-119124) with other animals?”  

“Same for me, I usually walk.”

The two of them kept walking, on the lookout for anything interesting. Finally, the spied another couple. The way said couple held hands was different, more like a hug. They looked rather intimate. It was as if their seniors in love were giving them a pointer.

“M-My, should we also do that?”  

“Y-You don’t need to force yourself.”

At Orgo’s reply, Myuri came to a halt. She seemed to give the matter some serious thought.

Orgo swallowed. A conflict between wanting to hold hands in that manner and the fear of losing control due to that was raging within him.

Myuri seemed to come to a conclusion.

“O-Orgo… Could you…”  

“S-Sure.”

He held out his hand towards her. She took his big, rugged appendage into her own slender one and hugged his arm.

“L-Like this?”  

“I-I-I-I think so.”

For the two of them, this was an act of bravery. Orgo tried to hide his blush, while Myuri got so embarrassed by hugging him like the other couple, she seemed to reach the other side and calm down.

“Orgo… you have not been neglecting your training.”  

“Course I haven’t. I’m a swordsman.”  

“Somehow, this feels nostalgic.”

She almost unconsciously tightened her hold. Among their acquaintances, the tenderness of her chest was only second to Alim’s, which Orgo now keenly felt.

“For some reason, hugging while holding hands seems to have a calming effect.”  

“W-We did hug this morning, right?”  

“…You are right! But back then, it happened practically unconsciously. Holding you tight as your girlfriend… eh-heh-heh, it feels nice.”

Her unusual behavior made him blush even more. The two of them side by side, their bodies pushed close together. He didn’t even realize that this fulfilled the quota he had set himself for that date.

“…Orgo.”  

“Wh-What is it?”  

“I would like my chest to be a bit bigger, after all.”  

“Nah, I don’t care about that.”  

“It vexes me how it does not feel all squishy when I hug you.”  

“S-Squishy…?”

It actually it did feel so, but he couldn’t say that out loud.

After looking a little sullen for a moment, she seemed to change her mind, showing a bright expression as she hugged him again.

“That reminds me. In the past, you often carried me on your back, did you not, Orgo? The feeling resembles those times.”  

“Now that you mention it, we did that.”

Right now, this was no longer something he thought he could do nonchalantly.

She seemed to remember something else.

“…Do you still have that old scar? Or was it healed when Alim brought us back?”  

“For some reason, it’s still there.”  

“I see…”

She ended her embrace and looked up at his face while still holding his hand. He couldn’t look anywhere but into her eyes, which were shining strongly with a hint of melancholy.

“I understood when I boldly decided to hug you. I love you, Orgo. Probably since back then.”  

“…Right.”  

“Heh-heh, I read a book about love the other day.”

The though of her having read similar books as him, made him sigh inwardly. She was still gazing at him.

“Could you bend down a bit?”  

“You want me to bend down?”

He did as she had asked him to. She then cupped his face with her free hand, gently pulling it closer until he felt a soft sensation on his lips.

“…This was the first for both of us, was it not?”  

“…Yes.”

The couple continued their date, now walking side by side.

#### Footnotes:

1. The verb 掛け合わせる used in the original is closer to “crossbreed” than “mingle”. Context makes the latter more probable, though it is possible that she’s so much of an airhead, she’s wondering whether a bird can produce offspring with a horse

# Side Story 24 – Seinforce’s Date – 4 (Ruin PoV)

After finishing lunch, Ruin and Lilo went back to wandering through the park.

“It’s surprising how many couples there are.”  

“Well, I think that’s the case for all big parks in the city.”  

“…Hey, Ruin,” Lilo said, as she observed one of the couples. “They all have their finger intertwined.”  

“Now that you mention it…”

He looked at her hand. When he saw her face and expression, he knew what he had to do and resolved himself not to miss this chance.

“In that case, should we also hold hands like that?”  

“…Yeah, let’s.”

He touched her hand with his fingers. She entwined her own with his.

“Doing stuff like this was so much easier when we were little.”  

“It’s because we’re now dating.”  

“Exactly, it makes a huge difference.”

While they were left bewildered that merely holding hands would fluster them this much, they did their best of savoring the feeling.

“So, where should we go next?”  

“I know the perfect place for a date in this park… Come on, it’s over there.”

Where Ruin was pointing stood a large tent. It was the venue of a theater troupe.

“True enough, I overheard several Maids who have boyfriends mention that this is a great place for a date.”  

“Same here. Shall we go in?”  

“Alright. Though I have no idea what the play is about or how good it is. I’ve seen lots of couples enter earlier… so we probably won’t feel out of place.”  

“That’s fine.”

The two of them paid the entry fee and went into the tent. Ruin paid for both himself and Myuri.

“Thank you. But just because you’re a prince doesn’t mean you have to treat me… you already paid for lunch.”  

“Well, I keep hearing that it’s expected for the man to pay during dates. It’s our first one, so that’s not a bad thing, right?”  

“I guess people do say that… I won’t decline in that case.”

They kept chatting while looking for their seats. In the tent, there were couples wherever they looked, and the number of people who seemed to be by themselves were in the single digits.

“Do you know what kind of play they show?”  

“Currently, it’s a love story between a nobleman and a peasant woman living in poverty.”  

“Oh, that would explain why there are so many couples here.”  

“…Looks like it’ll start soon.”

The play started with the sound of drums.

It was the scene where the supposed nobleman and the supposed destitute woman, who was wearing ragged clothes, met. Ruin and Lilo kept talking, keeping their voices low so they wouldn’t bother the people around them.

“Were there parts of the city where people used to be this poor?”  

“At this point, there shouldn’t be anyone living in this country who has to worry whether they’ll be able to eat tomorrow. Father and the king before him worked tirelessly to overhaul the system, Mr. Uruto took care of the slave trade, and thanks to Alim, we managed to eliminate the rampant crime in backstreet alleys and such.”  

“That’s true… I suppose it could be based on another country.”

It was exactly because they were a noblewoman and a prince that they couldn’t help but ponder these political issues. The two of them continued watching the play.

_“Why? Why should you be different from me?”_  

_“Even though we were born under the same sky! Why us?”_

As the middle part of the play came to its end, the two of them watched with teary eyes.

“A-Amazing, I never thought a play could move me this much.”  

“J-Just how will it end?”

The play entered its final part. It was a scene where the protagonists met in secret.

_“Somehow, if you hold my hand… I feel safe.”_

The moment that sentence was spoken, the couples in the audience simultaneously took each other’s hands and the girlfriends nuzzled closer against the boyfriends.

“Eh, what’s this now?”  

“This apparently happens all the time.”  

“I-I see. In that case…”

Just like the people around them, Lilo took Ruin’s hand and nestled close to him.

_(Uh… so soft)_  

Although Ruin got distracted by his childhood friend’s voluptuous assets pushing against him, he still managed to focus on the play.

“Uhm, how long should we stay like this?”  

“Until the people around us stop, I guess?”  

“Isn’t it too stifling for you, Ruin?”  

“It should be fine, even if we stay like this until the play ends.”  

“Are you sure? Alright.”

Lilo also seemed to be fine with their current position, so she stayed close to him, holding his hand. In the end, they kept like this for another 40 minutes.

It was the play’s finale.

_“I don’t care who you are! I love you!”_  

_“I also love you!”_

The couple was then officially wed, after they managed to coax their parents onto the stage. The two actors hugged and kissed. The moment they did, all the couples in the audience also hugged and went for a kiss.

“Wha- they’re kissing…!?”  

“Ha-ha-ha, I didn’t see that coming.”  

“…Ruin, what do you want to do?”

He was perplexed for a moment by her question. Before he knew it, he was holding her shoulders, and they were looking at each other.

“Are you sure?”  

“Yeah, though it is my first kiss…”  

“Same here.”  

“Eh-heh-heh, I knew that… mh.”  

“Hm.”

---

**TL notes:**  

Thus end the date side stories of volume 19.

These two dates in parallel could’ve been a good chance to show different approaches. For example, Orgo and Myuri are both rather insecure and thus keeping closer to typical date norms (like the man paying or the question whether to imitate other couples) while Ruin and Lilo are much more relaxed and could put their own spin on things. Sadly, this didn’t happen, and we got pretty much the same on both sides. Again.
